~~~java
    //æˆå‘˜å˜é‡
    private String name;
    private int age;

    //æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•
    Student3() {
    }

    Student3(String name, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }

    //æˆå‘˜æ–¹æ³•ï¼šå…¬å…±çš„setXxx()å’ŒgetXxx()ï¼Œä»¥åŠç±»å…¶ä»–çš„æ–¹æ³•
    public void setName(String name) {
        this.name = name;
    }

    public String getName() {
        return this.name;
    }

    public void setAge(int age) {
        this.age = age;
    }

    public int getAge() {
        return this.age;
    }

    //showæ–¹æ³•
    public void show() {
        System.out.println("å§“åï¼š" + this.name);
        System.out.println("å¹´é¾„ï¼š" + this.age);
    }
}
~~~

##### 2ã€é¢å‘å¯¹è±¡çš„ç»ƒä¹ 

###### 2.1ã€å®šä¹‰ä¸€ä¸ªç±»Demo,å…¶ä¸­å®šä¹‰ä¸€ä¸ªæ±‚ä¸¤ä¸ªæ•°æ®å’Œçš„æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œå®šä¹‰ä¸€ä¸ªæµ‹è¯•äº†Testï¼Œè¿›è¡Œæµ‹è¯•

~~~Java
class Demo1 {
    //æˆå‘˜å˜é‡
    private int a;
    private int b;

    //æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•
    public Demo1() {
    }

    public Demo1(int a, int b) {
        this.a = a;
        this.b = b;
    }

    //æˆå‘˜æ–¹æ³•ï¼š
    public int getA() {
        return a;
    }

    public void setA(int a) {
        this.a = a;
    }

    public int getB() {
        return b;
    }

    public void setB(int b) {
        this.b = b;
    }

    public int sum() {
        return a + b;
    }

    public void show() {
        System.out.println("a: " + a);
        System.out.println("b: " + b);
    }
}


public class FengZhuangTest1 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
//        Demo1 demo1 = new Demo1();
////        System.out.println(demo1.fun1());
//        System.out.println(demo1.fun(12,34));

        Demo1 demo1 = new Demo1(12, 13);
        System.out.println(demo1.sum());

    }
}
~~~

###### 2.2ã€å®šä¹‰ä¸€ä¸ªé•¿æ–¹å½¢ç±»,å®šä¹‰ æ±‚å‘¨é•¿å’Œé¢ç§¯çš„æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œç„¶åå®šä¹‰ä¸€ä¸ªæµ‹è¯•äº†Test2ï¼Œè¿›è¡Œæµ‹è¯•

~~~Java
class Rectangle {
    private int length;
    private int width;

    public Rectangle() {
    }

    public Rectangle(int length, int width) {
        this.length = length;
        this.width = width;
    }

    public int getLength() {
        return length;
    }

    public void setLength(int length) {
        this.length = length;
    }

    public int getWidth() {
        return width;
    }

    public void setWidth(int width) {
        this.width = width;
    }

    public int getPerimeter() {
        return (length + width) * 2;
    }

    public int getSize() {
        return length * width;
    }

    public void show() {
        System.out.println("é•¿ä¸ºï¼š" + length);
        System.out.println("å®½ä¸ºï¼š" + width);
        System.out.println("å‘¨é•¿ä¸ºï¼š" + getPerimeter());
        System.out.println("é¢ç§¯ä¸ºï¼š" + getSize());
    }
}

public class FengZhuangTest2 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Rectangle rectangle = new Rectangle(10, 5);
        rectangle.show();
    }
}
~~~

##### 3ã€staticå…³é”®å­—

> ```java
> javaä¸­æä¾›äº†ä¸€ä¸ªå…³é”®å­—ï¼Œå¯ä»¥å°†å˜é‡å˜æˆç±»å˜é‡(å…±äº«å˜é‡)ï¼Œè¿™ä¸ªå…³é”®å­—ï¼šstatic é™æ€çš„
> 
> è¢«staticä¿®é¥°çš„æˆå‘˜ï¼Œä¼šè¢«è¯¥ç±»æ‰€æœ‰çš„å¯¹è±¡å…±äº«

~~~java
class Person {
    private String name;
    private int age;
    private static String nationality;

    public Person() {
    }

    public Person(String name, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }

    public Person(String name, int age, String nationality) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
        this.nationality = nationality;
    }

    public String getName() {
        return name;
    }

    public void setName(String name) {
        this.name = name;
    }

    public int getAge() {
        return age;
    }

    public void setAge(int age) {
        this.age = age;
    }

    public String getNationality() {
        return nationality;
    }

    public void setNationality(String nationality) {
        this.nationality = nationality;
    }

    public void show() {
        System.out.println("å§“åï¼š" + name + ", å¹´é¾„ï¼š" + age + ", å›½ç±ï¼š" + nationality);
    }
}

public class StaticDemo1 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        //åˆ›å»ºå‡ ä¸ªå¯¹è±¡ï¼Œéƒ½æ˜¯ä¸­å›½äºº
        Person p1 = new Person("èƒ¡æ­Œ", 40, "ä¸­å›½");
        Person p2 = new Person("é‚“ç´«æ£‹", 30);
        Person p3 = new Person("è–›ä¹‹è°¦", 40);

        p1.show();
        p2.show();
        p3.show();
    }
}
~~~

###### 3.1æ³¨æ„äº‹é¡¹

> ```java
> static: é™æ€çš„ï¼Œå¯ä»¥ä¿®é¥°æˆå‘˜å˜é‡ï¼Œæˆå‘˜æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œä»£ç å—
> staticä¿®é¥°æˆå‘˜å˜é‡çš„æ³¨æ„äº‹é¡¹ï¼š

~~~java
        this.age = age;

        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
        this.nationality = nationality;

        System.out.println("å§“åï¼š" + name + ", å¹´é¾„ï¼š" + age + ", å›½ç±ï¼š" + nationality);
    }
~~~

##### 4ã€mainæ–¹æ³•

~~~Java

/*
    public: æœ€å¤§çš„æƒé™
    class: è¡¨ç¤ºä¸€ä¸ªç±»ï¼Œæ˜¯javaä¸­çš„åŸºæœ¬å•ä½

public class MainDemo {
    /*
        public: æœ€å¤§çš„æƒé™,å› ä¸ºmainæ–¹æ³•å°†æ¥è¦è¢«JVMæ‰€è¯†åˆ«è°ƒç”¨ï¼Œæƒé™è¦æœ€å¤§
        static: é™æ€çš„ï¼Œå°†æ¥å¯ä»¥ç›´æ¥ç±»è°ƒç”¨
        void: æ— è¿”å›å€¼çš„æ„æ€ï¼Œè¿”å›ç»™JVMæ¯«æ— æ„ä¹‰
        main: æ˜¯JVMæ‰€è¯†åˆ«å…¥å£çš„åå­—
        String[]: å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸€ç»´æ•°ç»„ç±»å‹
        args: å½¢å‚çš„åå­—
     */
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        for (int i = 0; i < args.length; i++) {
            System.out.println(args[i]);
        }
    }
}
~~~

~~~java
        int a = 30;
        System.out.println(a); // è·å–çš„æ˜¯å½“å‰æ–¹æ³•ä¸­çš„å±€éƒ¨å˜é‡aï¼š30
~~~

###### 6.8ã€ç»§æ‰¿-çŒ«ç‹—æ¡ˆä¾‹

~~~Java
class Animal {
    String name;
    int age;

    public Animal() {
    }

    public Animal(String name, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }

    public void eat() {
        System.out.println("åƒ");
    }

    public void sleep() {
        System.out.println("ç¡");
    }

    public void show() {
        System.out.println("å§“åï¼š" + name);
        System.out.println("å¹´é¾„ï¼š" + age);
    }
}

class Cat extends Animal {
    public Cat() {
    }

    public Cat(String name, int age) {
        super(name, age);
    }

    @Override
    public void eat() {
~~~

~~~java
    @Override
    public void fun1(){
        System.out.println("è¿™æ˜¯é‡å†™åçš„fun1æ–¹æ³•");
    }

    public void show1(){
        System.out.println("hello world");
    }
~~~

###### 8.6ã€å¤šæ€-è€å¸ˆæ¡ˆä¾‹

~~~Java
package com.shujia.day08.ketang;

/*
    è€å¸ˆæ¡ˆä¾‹
    å…·ä½“äº‹ç‰©ï¼š29æœŸè€å¸ˆï¼Œ28æœŸè€å¸ˆ
    å…±æ€§ï¼šå§“åï¼Œå¹´é¾„ï¼Œè®²è¯¾ã€‚

 */
abstract class Teacher{
    private String name;
    private int age;

    public Teacher() {
    }

    public Teacher(String name, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }

    public String getName() {
        return name;
    }

    public void setName(String name) {
        this.name = name;
    }

    public int getAge() {
        return age;
    }

    public void setAge(int age) {
        this.age = age;
    }

    //å°†è®²è¯¾çš„æ–¹æ³•è®¾ç½®ä¸ºæŠ½è±¡æ–¹æ³•
    public abstract void teach();

}

//åˆ›å»º28æœŸè€å¸ˆç±»
class Teacher28 extends Teacher{
    public Teacher28() {
    }

    public Teacher28(String name, int age) {
        super(name, age);
    }

    @Override
    public void teach() {
        System.out.println("hiveæ•™å­¦");
    }

    public void chaoGu(){
        System.out.println("ç‚’è‚¡");
    }
}

class Teacher29 extends Teacher{
    public Teacher29() {
    }

    public Teacher29(String name, int age) {
        super(name, age);
    }

    @Override
    public void teach() {
        System.out.println("javaæ•™å­¦");
    }

    public void playGame(){
        System.out.println("æ‰“æ¸¸æˆ");
    }
}


public class DuoTaiTest {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        //åˆ›å»º28æœŸçš„è€å¸ˆ
        Teacher t1 = new Teacher28("ç«¥å“¥",18);  // æŠ½è±¡å¤šæ€
        t1.teach();
//        t1.chaoGu();
        //å‘ä¸‹è½¬å‹
        Teacher28 t28 = (Teacher28) t1;
        t28.chaoGu();
        System.out.println("================================");
        Teacher t2 = new Teacher29("xiaohu",19);
        t2.teach();
//        t2.playGame();
        //å‘ä¸‹è½¬å‹
        Teacher29 t29 = (Teacher29) t2;
        t29.playGame();


    }
}
~~~

~~~Java
class Outer {
    public int num = 10;
    class Inner {
        public int num = 20;
        public void show() {
            int num = 30;
            System.out.println(num); // 30
            System.out.println(this.num); // 20
//            System.out.println(new Outer().num); // 10
            System.out.println(Outer.this.num); //
        }
    }
}


public class InnerClassTest1 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Outer.Inner oi = new Outer().new Inner();
        oi.show();
    }
}
~~~

### ç¬¬å››ç« Javaä¸­å¸¸ç”¨çš„ç±»

#### Objectç±»

##### 1ã€æ¦‚è¿°

> ç±»å±‚æ¬¡ç»“æ„çš„æ ¹ç±»
> æ‰€æœ‰ç±»éƒ½ç›´æ¥æˆ–è€…é—´æ¥çš„ç»§æ‰¿è‡ªè¯¥ç±»

##### 2ã€æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•

> public Object()

##### 3ã€æˆå‘˜æ–¹æ³•

###### 3.1ã€æ¡ˆä¾‹1

~~~Java
		public int hashCode() è¿”å›å¯¹è±¡çš„å“ˆå¸Œç å€¼ã€‚
        public final Class getClass() è·å–ä¸€ä¸ªç±»å¯¹åº”çš„Classå¯¹è±¡
        public String toString() è¾“å‡ºä¸€ä¸ªå¯¹è±¡ï¼Œå®é™…ä¸Šè¾“å‡ºçš„æ˜¯å¯¹è±¡è°ƒç”¨çš„toString()æ–¹æ³•
         ä¸€ä¸ªæ ‡å‡†ç±»çš„æœ€ç»ˆå†™æ³•ï¼š
        1ã€æˆå‘˜å˜é‡ç§æœ‰åŒ–
        2ã€æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•ï¼ˆæ— å‚/æ‰€æœ‰å‚æ•°ï¼‰
        3ã€getXxx()å’ŒsetXxx()
        4ã€toString()
~~~

~~~Java
class Student {
    //åŒ…å«äº†ç»§æ‰¿è‡ªObjectç±»çš„æ–¹æ³•
    String name;
    int age;

    public Student() {
    }

    public Student(String name, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return "Student{" +
                "name='" + name + '\'' +
                ", age=" + age +
                '}';
    }
}

public class ObjectDemo1 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Student s1 = new Student();
//        System.out.println(s1.hashCode()); // 1163157884
//
//        Student s2 = new Student();
//        System.out.println(s2.hashCode()); // 1956725890

        Class c1 = s1.getClass();
        System.out.println(c1.hashCode()); // 1163157884


        Student s2 = new Student();
        Class c2 = s2.getClass();
        System.out.println(c2.hashCode()); // 1163157884
        System.out.println(c2); // class com.shujia.day10.Student

        System.out.println(s2.toString()); // com.shujia.day10.Student@74a14482
        //getClass().getName() + '@' + Integer.toHexString(hashCode())
        System.out.println(s2.getClass().getName()); // com.shujia.day10.Student+'@'+74a14482
        System.out.println(Integer.toHexString(1956725890)); // å°†æ•´æ•°å€¼è½¬æˆ16è¿›åˆ¶å­—ç¬¦ä¸² 74a14482

        System.out.println(s1); // com.shujia.day10.Student@1540e19d
        Student s3 = new Student("å°è™", 18);
        System.out.println(s3); // com.shujia.day10.Student@677327b6 Student{name='å°è™', age=18}
        //æˆ‘ä»¬æ­£å¸¸å¼€å‘ä¸­ï¼Œè¾“å‡ºä¸€ä¸ªå¯¹è±¡ï¼Œå®é™…ä¸Šæˆ‘ä»¬æƒ³è¦è¾“å‡ºå¯¹è±¡çš„æˆå‘˜å˜é‡å€¼çš„æƒ…å†µï¼Œè€Œä¸æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªåœ°å€å€¼
        //æˆ‘ä»¬è‡ªå·±çš„ç±»ä¸­é‡å†™ç»§æ‰¿è‡ªObjectç±»ä¸­çš„toString()æ–¹æ³•å°±å¯ä»¥äº†
        //è‡ªåŠ¨ç”Ÿæˆå³å¯


    }
}
~~~

###### 3.2ã€æ¡ˆä¾‹2

```Java
   public boolean equals(Object obj)
		protected void finalize() ç”¨äºåƒåœ¾å›æ”¶çš„
		protected Object clone()
```

~~~Java
package com.shujia.day10;

import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Scanner;

/*
    public boolean equals(Object obj)
    protected void finalize() ç”¨äºåƒåœ¾å›æ”¶çš„
    protected Object clone()

 */
class Student2 extends Object{
    String name;
    int age;

    public Student2() {
    }

    public Student2(String name, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }

    /*
        public boolean equals(Object obj) {
            return (this == obj);
        }
     */

    @Override
    public boolean equals(Object o) {
        if (this == o) return true;
        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) return false;
        Student2 student2 = (Student2) o;
        return age == student2.age && Objects.equals(name, student2.name);
    }
}

public class ObjectDemo2 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        //åˆ›å»ºç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå­¦ç”Ÿå¯¹è±¡
        Student2 s1 = new Student2("ä¸ä¹‰æ°", 17);

        //åˆ›å»ºç¬¬äºŒä¸ªå­¦ç”Ÿå¯¹è±¡
        Student2 s2 = new Student2("ä¸ä¹‰æ°", 17);

        //==æ¯”è¾ƒå¼•ç”¨æ•°æ®ç±»å‹çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œæ¯”è¾ƒçš„æ˜¯åœ°å€å€¼
        System.out.println(s1==s2); // false
        /*
         public boolean equals(Object obj) { //Object obj = new Student2("ä¸ä¹‰æ°", 17);
            //this -- s1
            //obj -- s2
            return (this == obj);
         }
         */
        //Objectç±»ä¸­çš„equalsæ–¹æ³•é»˜è®¤æ¯”è¾ƒçš„æ˜¯å¯¹è±¡çš„åœ°å€å€¼
        System.out.println(s1.equals(s2)); // false // true
        //è¦æƒ³æ¯”è¾ƒä¸¤ä¸ªå¯¹è±¡ä¸­çš„æˆå‘˜å˜é‡å€¼æ˜¯å¦ä¸€æ ·
        //åªéœ€è¦è‡ªå·±å¯¹è±¡æ‰€å±ç±»ä¸­é‡å†™equalsæ–¹æ³•ï¼Œæ”¹å†™æˆæ¯”è¾ƒæˆå‘˜å˜é‡å€¼å°±å¯ä»¥äº†
        //è‡ªåŠ¨ç”Ÿæˆå³å¯

        //å­—ç¬¦ä¸²çš„æ¯”è¾ƒ String
        String str1 = "hello"; // å­˜æ”¾åœ¨å†…å­˜ä¸­çš„æ–¹æ³•åŒºçš„å¸¸é‡æ± ä¸­
//        System.out.println(str1.hashCode());
        System.out.println(System.identityHashCode(str1)); // 1163157884
        String str2 = new String("hello"); // å­˜æ”¾åœ¨å †å†…å­˜ä¸­ï¼Œå®é™…ä¸ŠæŒ‡å‘çš„ä¾æ—§æ˜¯å¸¸é‡æ± ä¸­

        System.out.println(System.identityHashCode(str2)); // 1956725890
        System.out.println(str1==str2); // false
        System.out.println(str1.equals(str2)); // true


    }
}
~~~

~~~Java
package com.shujia.day10;

/*
    protected Object clone() æ‹·è´

    æµ…æ‹·è´  âˆš
    æ·±æ‹·è´

    é¦–å…ˆï¼Œå¦‚æœæ­¤å¯¹è±¡çš„ç±»ä¸å®ç°æ¥å£Cloneable ï¼Œåˆ™æŠ›å‡ºCloneNotSupportedException ã€‚
    Cloneableä¸­ä»€ä¹ˆæˆå‘˜éƒ½æ²¡æœ‰ï¼Œè¿™æ ·çš„æ¥å£ï¼Œåœ¨javaä¸­ç§°ä¹‹ä¸ºæ ‡è®°æ¥å£

 */

class Demo {
    int a = 20;
}

class Student3 implements Cloneable {
    String name;
    int age;
    Demo demo;

    public Student3() {
    }

    public Student3(String name, int age, Demo demo) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
        this.demo = demo;
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return "Student3{" +
                "name='" + name + '\'' +
                ", age=" + age +
                '}';
    }

    @Override
    protected Object clone() throws CloneNotSupportedException {
        return super.clone();
    }
//    @Override
//    protected Object clone() throws CloneNotSupportedException {
//        return super.clone();
//    }
}

public class ObjectDemo3 {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Demo demo = new Demo();

        Student3 s1 = new Student3("å°èŠ±", 18, demo);
//        System.out.println(s1); // Student3{name='å°èŠ±', age=18}
        System.out.println(s1.demo); // com.shujia.day10.Demo@4554617c

        Object o = s1.clone();
//        System.out.println(s1 == o); // false
//        System.out.println(o); // Student3{name='å°èŠ±', age=18}
        Student3 s = (Student3) o;
        System.out.println(s.demo); // com.shujia.day10.Demo@4554617c


    }
}
~~~

#### Scannerç±»

##### 1ã€æ¦‚è¿°

> JDK5ä»¥åç”¨äºè·å–ç”¨æˆ·çš„é”®ç›˜è¾“å…¥

##### 2ã€æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•

> ```java
> Scanner(InputStream source)  æ„é€ ä¸€ä¸ªæ–°çš„ Scanner ï¼Œäº§ç”Ÿä»æŒ‡å®šè¾“å…¥æµæ‰«æçš„å€¼ã€‚
> InputStream å­—èŠ‚æµ
> ```

##### 3ã€æˆå‘˜æ–¹æ³•

> ```java
> next() è·å–å­—ç¬¦ä¸²
> public String nextLine() è·å–å­—ç¬¦ä¸² å¯ä»¥æ¥æ”¶æ¢è¡Œç¬¦
> nextInt() è·å–æ•´æ•°
> 
> public boolean hasNextInt() åˆ¤æ–­ç®¡é“ä¸­çš„ä¸‹ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°æ®æ˜¯å¦æ˜¯æ•´æ•°
> ```

~~~java
public class ScannerDemo1 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
        System.out.println("è¯·è¾“å…¥ä¸€ä¸ªæ•´æ•°ï¼š");
        int number = 0;
        Scanner sc1 = null;
        if(sc.hasNextInt()){
            number = sc.nextInt();
        }else {
            sc1 = new Scanner(System.in);
            System.out.println("è¯·è¾“å…¥ä¸€ä¸ªæ•´æ•°ï¼š");
            number = sc1.nextInt();
        }

        System.out.println("è¯·è¾“å…¥ä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼š");
//        String s1 = sc.next();
        String s1 = sc1.next();
        System.out.println("--------------------------");
        System.out.println(s1);
        System.out.println(number);

    }
}
~~~

#### Stringç±»

##### 1ã€æ¦‚è¿°

> ```java
> String: å­—ç¬¦ä¸² ç”±è‹¥å¹²ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ç»„æˆçš„å­—ç¬¦åºåˆ—ï¼Œæ•´ä½“å«åšå­—ç¬¦ä¸²
> ç‰¹ç‚¹ï¼š
>     1ã€ä¸€æ—¦è¢«åˆ›å»ºï¼Œå°±ä¸èƒ½è¢«æ”¹å˜
>     2ã€Javaç¨‹åºä¸­çš„æ‰€æœ‰å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ–‡å­—ï¼ˆä¾‹å¦‚"abc" ï¼‰éƒ½è¢«å®ç°ä¸ºæ­¤ç±»çš„å®ä¾‹ã€‚
>     3ã€å› ä¸ºStringå¯¹è±¡æ˜¯ä¸å¯å˜çš„ï¼Œå®ƒä»¬å¯ä»¥è¢«å…±äº«ï¼ˆå¸¸é‡æ± ï¼‰
>     4ã€å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å¯ä»¥è¢«çœ‹ä½œä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦æ•°ç»„
> ```

##### 2ã€æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•

> ```java
> Stringç±»çš„æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•ï¼š
>     public String()
>     public String(byte[] bytes)
>     public String(byte[] bytes,int offset,int length)
>     public String(char[] value)
>     public String(char[] value,int offset,int count)
>     public String(String original)
> ```

###### 2.1ã€æ¡ˆä¾‹

~~~Java
public class StringDemo2 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s7 = "hello";

        //public String()
        String s1 = new String(); // ç›¸å½“äºåˆ›å»ºä¸€ä¸ªç©ºçš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²
        System.out.println("s1: " + s1); // Stringç±»é‡å†™äº†toString()æ–¹æ³•

        //public String(byte[] bytes) å°†å­—èŠ‚æ•°ç»„è½¬åŒ–æˆå­—ç¬¦ä¸²
        byte[] arr = {97, 98, 99, 100, 101, 102};
        String s2 = new String(arr);
        System.out.println("s2: " + s2); // "abcdef"

        //public String(byte[] bytes,int index,int length) å°†å­—èŠ‚æ•°ç»„çš„ä¸€éƒ¨åˆ†è½¬æˆå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œå…¶ä¸­çš„indexè¡¨ç¤ºç´¢å¼•ï¼Œlengthè¡¨ç¤ºè½¬æˆå­—ç¬¦ä¸²çš„ä¸ªæ•°
        String s3 = new String(arr, 2, 3);
        System.out.println("s3: " + s3);

        //public String(char[] value)  å°†å­—ç¬¦æ•°ç»„è½¬æˆå­—ç¬¦ä¸²
        char[] arr2 = {'æˆ‘', 'çˆ±', 'ä¸­', 'å›½'};
        String s4 = new String(arr2);
        System.out.println("s4: " + s4);

        //public String(char[] value,int index,int count) å°†å­—ç¬¦æ•°ç»„çš„ä¸€éƒ¨åˆ†è½¬æˆå­—ç¬¦ä¸²
        String s5 = new String(arr2, 1, 2);
        System.out.println("s5: " + s5);

        //public String(String original)
        String s6 = new String("java");
        System.out.println("s6: " + s6);

    }
}
~~~

##### Stringç±»çš„ä¸»è¦åŠŸèƒ½

###### 1ã€åˆ¤æ–­åŠŸèƒ½

> ```java
> boolean equals(Object obj)
> boolean equalsIgnoreCase(String str)//å¿½ç•¥å¤§å°å†™
> boolean contains(String str)//åˆ¤æ–­æ˜¯å¦åŒ…å«æŸä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²
> boolean startsWith(String str)//ä»¥ä»€ä¹ˆå¼€å¤´
> boolean endsWith(String str) //ä»¥ä»€ä¹ˆç»“å°¾
> boolean isEmpty()//æ˜¯å¦ä¸ºç©º
> ```

~~~java
public class StringDemo3 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s1 = "hello WoRLd";
        String s2 = "Hello World";

        //boolean equals(Object obj) åˆ¤æ–­ä¸¤ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²å†…å®¹æ˜¯å¦ç›¸åŒ
        System.out.println(s1.equals(s2)); // false

        //boolean equalsIgnoreCase(String str)  åˆ¤æ–­ä¸¤ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²å†…å®¹æ˜¯å¦ç›¸åŒ,å¿½ç•¥å¤§å°å†™æ¯”è¾ƒ
        System.out.println(s1.equalsIgnoreCase(s2)); // true

        //boolean contains(String str) åˆ¤æ–­ä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­æ˜¯å¦åŒ…å«å¦ä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²
        System.out.println(s1.contains("o World")); // false

        //boolean startsWith(String str) åˆ¤æ–­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ˜¯å¦ä»¥æŸä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²å¼€å¤´
        System.out.println(s1.startsWith("hew")); // false

        //boolean endsWith(String str) åˆ¤æ–­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ˜¯å¦ä»¥æŸä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ç»“å°¾
        System.out.println(s1.endsWith("Rld")); // false

        //boolean isEmpty() åˆ¤æ–­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ˜¯å¦ä¸ºç©ºå­—ç¬¦ä¸²
        s1 = "";

        System.out.println(s1.isEmpty()); // false
    }
}
~~~

###### 2ã€è·å–åŠŸèƒ½

> ```java
> int length()
> char charAt(int index)
> int indexOf(int ch)
> int indexOf(String str)
> int indexOf(int ch,int fromIndex)
> int indexOf(String str,int fromIndex)

~~~java
public class StringDemo4 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s1 = "hello WoeRLd";

        //int length() è·å–å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­çš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸ªæ•°
        System.out.println(s1.length());

        //char charAt(int index) æ ¹æ®ç´¢å¼•è·å–ç´¢å¼•å¯¹åº”çš„å­—ç¬¦
        System.out.println(s1.charAt(0)); // StringIndexOutOfBoundsException

        //int indexOf(int ch) è·å–å­—ç¬¦çš„ä½ç½®
        //101--ASCIIç ï¼še
        //åˆ¤æ–­'e'ç¬¬ä¸€æ¬¡å‡ºç°åœ¨å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­çš„ä½ç½®ç´¢å¼•
        System.out.println(s1.indexOf(200)); // -1

        //int indexOf(String str) è·å–å°å­—ç¬¦ä¸²åœ¨å¤§å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­ç¬¬ä¸€æ¬¡å‡ºç°çš„ä½ç½®ï¼Œè¿”å›å°å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦çš„ä½ç½®ç´¢å¼•
        System.out.println(s1.indexOf("o Wo"));

        //int indexOf(int ch,int fromIndex) //ä»fromIndexä½ç½®å¼€å§‹æ‰¾ï¼Œå¦‚æœæ‰¾åˆ°è¿”å›è¯¥å­—ç¬¦åœ¨å¤§å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­çš„ä½ç½®ç´¢å¼•
        //"hello WoeRLd"
        System.out.println(s1.indexOf(101)); // 1
        System.out.println(s1.indexOf(101,4)); // 8

        //int indexOf(String str,int fromIndex)

        //String substring(int start) å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æˆªå– ä»startç´¢å¼•ä½ç½®æˆªå–ï¼Œä¸€ç›´åˆ°æœ«å°¾
        //"hello WoeRLd"
        System.out.println(s1.substring(3));

        //String substring(int start,int end) å­ä¸²å¼€å§‹äºæŒ‡å®šbeginIndexå¹¶å»¶ä¼¸åˆ°å­—ç¬¦ç´¢å¼•endIndex-1
        //[start,end)
        System.out.println(s1.substring(4,8));


    }
}
~~~

###### 3ã€è½¬æ¢åŠŸèƒ½

> ```java
> byte[] getBytes()
> char[] toCharArray()
> static String valueOf(char[] chs)
> static String valueOf(int i)
> String toLowerCase()
> String toUpperCase()
> String concat(String str)
> ```

~~~java
public class StringDemo5 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s1 = "æˆ‘çˆ±ä¸­å›½æˆ‘";

        //byte[] getBytes() å°†å­—ç¬¦ä¸²è½¬æ¢æˆå­—èŠ‚æ•°ç»„
        byte[] bytes = s1.getBytes();
//        System.out.println(bytes); // [B@4554617c
//        for (int i = 0; i < bytes.length; i++) {
//            System.out.println(bytes[i]);
//        }

        // char[] toCharArray() å°†å­—ç¬¦ä¸²è½¬æ¢æˆå­—ç¬¦æ•°ç»„
        char[] charArray = s1.toCharArray();
//        for (int i = 0; i < charArray.length; i++) {
//            System.out.println(charArray[i]);
//        }

        //static String valueOf(char[] chs) //å°†å­—ç¬¦æ•°ç»„è½¬æˆå­—ç¬¦ä¸²
        String s2 = String.valueOf(charArray);
        System.out.println(s1 == s2); // false

        //static String valueOf(int i)  å°†æ•°å€¼è½¬æˆå­—ç¬¦ä¸²  100-->"100"
        String s3 = String.valueOf(100);
        System.out.println(s3);

        //String toLowerCase()  è½¬å°å†™
        String s4 = "Hello WORLD";
        String s5 = s4.toLowerCase();
        System.out.println(s5);

        //String toUpperCase() è½¬å¤§å†™
        System.out.println(s5.toUpperCase());

        //String concat(String str) å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ‹¼æ¥
        System.out.println("s5: " + s5);
        String s6 = "s5: " + s5;
        String s7 = "s5: ".concat(s5);
        System.out.println(s6);
        System.out.println(s7);


    }
}
~~~

###### 4ã€å…¶ä»–åŠŸèƒ½

> ```java
> æ›¿æ¢åŠŸèƒ½
>     String replace(char old,char new)
>     String replace(String old,String new)
> å»é™¤å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸¤ç©ºæ ¼
>     String trim()
> æŒ‰å­—å…¸é¡ºåºæ¯”è¾ƒä¸¤ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²

~~~java
public class StringDemo6 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s1 = "Hello WorLD";

        System.out.println(s1);
        //String replace(char old,char new)  ä½¿ç”¨æ–°å­—ç¬¦æ›¿æ¢æ—§å­—ç¬¦
        System.out.println(s1.replace('o', '_'));

        //String replace(String old,String new) ä½¿ç”¨å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ›¿æ¢æ—§å­—ç¬¦ä¸²
        System.out.println(s1.replace("ll","æ•°åŠ ç§‘æŠ€"));

        //String trim() å»é™¤å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸¤è¾¹çš„ç©ºæ ¼
        String s2 = "  Hello WorLD  ";
        System.out.println(s2.trim());
        System.out.println(s2);


        //æ¯”è¾ƒä¸¤ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²å†…å®¹æ˜¯å¦ç›¸åŒï¼Œåœ¨javaä¸­æœ‰ä¸¤ç§æ–¹æ³•å¯ä»¥å®ç°
        //boolean equals(String s)
        String s3 = "hello";
        String s4 = "world";
        System.out.println(s3.equals(s4));
        //int compareTo(String str)
        System.out.println(s3.compareTo(s4)); // -15
        String s5 = "hel";
        System.out.println(s3.compareTo(s5)); // 2
        String s6 = "hello";
        System.out.println(s3.compareTo(s6)); // 0
    }
}
~~~

###### 1ã€æ¡ˆä¾‹1

> ```java
> ç»Ÿè®¡å¤§ä¸²ä¸­å°ä¸²å‡ºç°çš„æ¬¡æ•°
> ä¸¾ä¾‹ï¼šåœ¨å­—ç¬¦ä¸²â€ woaijavawozhenaijavawozhendeaijavawozhendehenaijavaxinbuxinwoaijavagunâ€ä¸­javaå‡ºç°äº†5æ¬¡
> 
> åˆ†æï¼š
>     1ã€å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨indexOf()æ–¹æ³•è·å–å°ä¸²ç¬¬ä¸€æ¬¡å‡ºç°çš„ä½ç½®
>     2ã€ä½¿ç”¨subString()æˆªå–æ¯æ¬¡javaçš„åç»­å‰©ä½™å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œç»§ç»­æŸ¥æ‰¾
>     3ã€å› ä¸ºä¸çŸ¥é“æ¬¡æ•°ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨whileå¾ªç¯

~~~java
public class StringTest3 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String bigStr = "woaijavawozhenaijavawozhendeaijavawozhendehenaijavaxinbuxinwoaijavagun";
        String str = "java";
        int count = 0;

        int i = bigStr.indexOf("java"); // 4 // 8
        while (i != -1) {
            count++;
            bigStr = bigStr.substring(i + str.length());
            i = bigStr.indexOf("java");
        }
        System.out.println("javaå­—ç¬¦ä¸²å…±å‡ºç°äº† " + count + "æ¬¡");
    }
}
~~~

###### 3ã€æ¡ˆä¾‹3

> ```java
> æŠŠæ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„æ•°æ®æŒ‰ç…§æŒ‡å®šä¸ªæ ¼å¼æ‹¼æ¥æˆä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²
> ä¸¾ä¾‹ï¼šint[] arr = {1,2,3}; è¾“å‡ºç»“æœï¼š[1, 2, 3]
> ```

~~~java
public class StringTest1 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        int[] arr = {1, 2, 3};

        String str = "[";
        for (int i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
            if (i == arr.length - 1) {
                str = str.concat(arr[i]+"]");
            }else {
                str = str.concat(arr[i]+",");
            }
        }

        System.out.println(str);
    }
}
~~~

#### StringBufferç±»

##### 1ã€æ¦‚è¿°

> ```java
> StringBuffer: å¯å˜çš„å­—ç¬¦åºåˆ—ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å¯ä»¥ç†è§£ä¸ºæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªå¯å˜çš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œçº¿ç¨‹å®‰å…¨

##### 2ã€æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•

> ```java
> public StringBuffer()
> public StringBuffer(int capacity)
> public StringBuffer(String str)

~~~java
public class StringBufferDemo1 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        // public StringBuffer()  åˆ›å»ºä¸€ä¸ªç©ºçš„StringBufferå®¹å™¨
        StringBuffer sb1 = new StringBuffer();
        // public int capacity() è¿”å›å½“å‰å®¹é‡ã€‚
        System.out.println(sb1.capacity()); // 16
        //public int length() è¿”å›é•¿åº¦ï¼ˆå­—ç¬¦æ•°ï¼‰ã€‚
        System.out.println(sb1.length()); // 0
        System.out.println("sb1: " + sb1); // StringBufferé‡å†™äº†toString()

        //public StringBuffer(int capacity) åˆ›å»ºæŒ‡å®šå¤§å°å®¹é‡çš„å®¹å™¨
        StringBuffer sb2 = new StringBuffer(20);
        System.out.println(sb2.capacity());
        System.out.println(sb2.length());

        //public StringBuffer(String str) åˆ›å»ºStringBufferçš„åŒæ—¶ï¼Œå†…éƒ¨å°±åŒ…å«äº†ä¸€ä¸ªåˆå§‹å­—ç¬¦ä¸²
        StringBuffer sb3 = new StringBuffer("hello");
        System.out.println("sb3: " + sb3);
        System.out.println(sb3.capacity()); // 21
        System.out.println(sb3.length()); // 5


    }
}
~~~

##### 3ã€ä¸»è¦åŠŸèƒ½

> ```java
> æ·»åŠ åŠŸèƒ½
>     public StringBuffer append(String str)
>     public StringBuffer insert(int offset,String str)
> åˆ é™¤åŠŸèƒ½
>     public StringBuffer deleteCharAt(int index)
>     public StringBuffer delete(int start,int end)
> æ›¿æ¢åŠŸèƒ½

~~~java
public class StringBufferDemo2 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        StringBuffer sb1 = new StringBuffer(); // 16
        System.out.println("sb1: " + sb1);

        System.out.println("---------------------------------");
        //public StringBuffer append(String str) è¿½åŠ 
        //æ— è®ºæ·»åŠ çš„æ˜¯ä»€ä¹ˆç±»å‹çš„å…ƒç´ å€¼ï¼Œåªè¦è¿›å…¥åˆ°StringBufferä¸­ï¼Œå®ƒå°±æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªä¸€ä¸ªçš„æ™®é€šå­—ç¬¦
        sb1.append("java")
                .append(100)
                .append(12.34)
                .append(true);
        System.out.println("sb1: " + sb1);
        //java10hello012.34true

        //public StringBuffer insert(int index,String str) åœ¨StringBufferå®¹å™¨ä¸­æŒ‡å®šä½ç½®æ·»åŠ å­—ç¬¦ä¸²
        sb1.insert(6,"hello");
        System.out.println("sb1: " + sb1);
//        System.out.println(sb1.capacity()); // 34
//        System.out.println(sb1.length());

        //public StringBuffer deleteCharAt(int index) åˆ é™¤æŒ‡å®šä½ç½®ç´¢å¼•ä¸Šçš„å­—ç¬¦
//        sb1.deleteCharAt(10);
//        System.out.println("sb1: " + sb1);

        //public StringBuffer delete(int start,int end) [start,end)
        //java10hello012.34true
//        sb1.delete(8,14);
//        System.out.println("sb1: " + sb1);

        //public StringBuffer replace(int start,int end,String str) [start,end)
        //java10hello012.34true
        sb1.replace(8,12,"æ•°åŠ ç§‘æŠ€");
        System.out.println("sb1: " + sb1);

        //public StringBuffer reverse() åè½¬
        StringBuffer sb2 = new StringBuffer("abcdef");
        System.out.println("sb2: "+sb2);
        sb2.reverse();
        System.out.println("sb2: "+sb2);


    }
}
~~~

~~~java
public class StringBufferDemo3 {

        StringBuffer sb = new StringBuffer("hello world");
~~~

##### 4ã€æ¡ˆä¾‹

###### 4.1ã€

> ```java
> Stringå’ŒStringBufferçš„ç›¸äº’è½¬æ¢
> 
> A<-->B
> ä»€ä¹ˆåœºæ™¯éœ€è¦åšè½¬æ¢æ“ä½œï¼š
> åœºæ™¯1ï¼šå¯ä»¥éœ€è¦ç”¨åˆ°å¦ä¸€ç§ç±»ä¸­çš„æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œæ¥æ–¹ä¾¿å¤„ç†æˆ‘ä»¬çš„éœ€æ±‚
> åœºæ™¯2ï¼šæ–¹æ³•ä¼ å‚
> ```

~~~java
public class StringBufferDemo1 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        //åˆ›å»ºä¸€ä¸ªStringå¯¹è±¡
        String s1 = "hello";
        System.out.println("s1: " + s1);

        //String-->StringBuffer
        //1ã€ä½¿ç”¨StringBufferæ„é€ æ–¹æ³•
        StringBuffer sb1 = new StringBuffer(s1);
        System.out.println("sb1: " + sb1);


        //StringBuffer-->String
        //1ã€toString()æ–¹æ³•
        StringBuffer sb2 = new StringBuffer("world");
        String s2 = sb2.toString();
        //2ã€æˆªå–
        String s3 = sb2.substring(0);

        System.out.println("--------------è½¬æ¢è°ƒç”¨å¦ä¸€ç§ç±»ä¸­çš„æ–¹æ³•æ¡ˆä¾‹-------------------");
        //Stringå¯¹è±¡å­—ç¬¦ä¸²é€†åº
        String s4 = "abcd";
        System.out.println("s4: "+s4);
        //å…ˆè½¬StringBuffer
        StringBuffer sb3 = new StringBuffer(s4);
        sb3.reverse();
        //å†è½¬å›å­—ç¬¦ä¸²Stringç±»å‹
        String s5 = sb3.toString();
        System.out.println("s5: "+s5);

    }
}
~~~

###### 4.2ã€

> ```java
> çœ‹ç¨‹åºå†™ç»“æœï¼š
>     Stringä½œä¸ºå‚æ•°ä¼ é€’
>     StringBufferä½œä¸ºå‚æ•°ä¼ é€’: å“ªä¸€ä¸ªStringBufferå¯¹è±¡è°ƒç”¨æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œå“ªä¸€ä¸ªå°±ä¼šæ”¹å˜
> ```

~~~java
public class StringBufferDemo2 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
//        String s1 = "hello";
//        String s2 = "world";
//        System.out.println("s1: " + s1 + ", s2: " + s2); // s1: hello,s2: world
//        change(s1, s2);
//        System.out.println("s1: " + s1 + ", s2: " + s2); // s1: hello,s2: world

        StringBuffer sb1 = new StringBuffer("hello");
        StringBuffer sb2 = new StringBuffer("world");
        System.out.println("sb1: " + sb1 + ",sb2: " + sb2); // sb1: hello,sb2: world
        change(sb1,sb2);
        System.out.println("sb1: " + sb1 + ",sb2: " + sb2); //sb1: hello,sb2: worldworld
    }

    public static void change(StringBuffer sb1,StringBuffer sb2){
        sb1 = sb2;
        sb2 = sb1.append(sb2); //
        System.out.println("sb1: " + sb1 + ",sb2: " + sb2); // sb1: worldworld,sb2: worldworld
    }


    public static void change(String s1, String s2) {
        s1 = s2; // s1: "world"  s2: "world"
        s2 = s1 + s2; // s1: "world" s2: "worldworld"
        System.out.println("s1: " + s1 + ", s2: " + s2); // s1: world,s2: worldworld
    }
}
~~~

###### 4.3ã€

> ```
> æŠŠæ•°ç»„æ‹¼æ¥æˆä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²
> ```

~~~Java
public class StringBufferTest1 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        int[] arr = {11, 22, 33, 44, 55};
        //åˆ›å»ºä¸€ä¸ªç©ºçš„StringBuffer
        StringBuffer sb = new StringBuffer();
        for (int i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
            sb.append(arr[i]);
        }
        String s = sb.toString();

        System.out.println("s: "+s);
    }
}
~~~

#### DateFormatç±»

##### 1ã€æ¦‚è¿°

> DateFormat æ˜¯æ—¥æœŸ/æ—¶é—´æ ¼å¼åŒ–å­ç±»çš„æŠ½è±¡ç±»ï¼Œå®ƒä»¥ä¸è¯­è¨€æ— å…³çš„æ–¹å¼æ ¼å¼åŒ–å¹¶è§£ææ—¥æœŸæˆ–æ—¶é—´ã€‚
> æ˜¯æŠ½è±¡ç±»ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨å…¶å­ç±»SimpleDateFormat

##### 2ã€SimpleDateFormatç±»çš„æˆå‘˜æ–¹æ³•å’Œæ„é€ æ–¹æ³•

~~~Java
package com.shujia.day11;

import com.shujia.day11.utils.DateUtil;

import java.text.SimpleDateFormat;
import java.util.Date;

/*
    æ—¥æœŸæ ¼å¼åŒ–ç±»ï¼šSimpleDateFormat

    æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•ï¼š
        public SimpleDateFormat(String pattern) yyyyå¹´MMæœˆddæ—¥ HHæ—¶mmåˆ†ssç§’

 */
public class SimpleDateFormatDemo {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        SimpleDateFormat sdf = new SimpleDateFormat("yyyyå¹´MMæœˆddæ—¥ HHæ—¶mmåˆ†ssç§’");

        Date date = new Date();
        System.out.println(date); // Mon Mar 04 15:06:31 CST 2024
//public final String format(Date date)å°†Dateç±»å‹çš„å€¼æ ¼å¼åŒ–æˆ‘ä»¬ç›®æ ‡çš„å½¢å¼
//public Date parse(String source) å°†Stringç±»å‹çš„æ ¼å¼è½¬æ¢ä¸ºDateæ ¼å¼

        String res1 = sdf.format(date); // å°†Dateç±»å‹çš„å€¼æ ¼å¼åŒ–æˆ‘ä»¬ç›®æ ‡çš„å½¢å¼
        System.out.println(res1);

        //éœ€æ±‚ï¼šå°†ä¸€ä¸ªæ—¶é—´æˆ³è½¬æˆæŒ‡å®šæ—¥æœŸæ ¼å¼ 1709535166924
        //æ—¶é—´æˆ³--Date--æ ¼å¼åŒ–
//        Date date1 = new Date(1709535166924L);
//        String res2 = sdf.format(date1);
//        System.out.println(res2);
        System.out.println(DateUtil.formatDate(1709535166924L));

    }
}
~~~

### ç¬¬äº”ç« é›†åˆ

> ```
> å›é¡¾ä¸€ä¸‹åˆ°ç›®å‰ä¸ºæ­¢ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬å­¦ä¹ è¿‡å“ªäº›å®¹å™¨
> æ•°ç»„ï¼šé•¿åº¦ä¸€æ—¦ç¡®å®šå°±ä¸èƒ½æ›´æ”¹ï¼Œå¯¹äºåŒä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ç»„ä¸­ï¼Œæ—¢å¯ä»¥æ˜¯å­˜æ”¾åŸºæœ¬æ•°æ®ç±»å‹å…ƒç´ çš„æ•°ç»„ï¼Œä¹Ÿå¯ä»¥æ˜¯å­˜æ”¾å¼•ç”¨æ•°æ®ç±»å‹æ•°ç»„

> æˆ‘ä»¬å­¦ä¹ ï¼Œæœ¬è´¨ä¸Šæ˜¯å­¦ä¹ ä¸åŒçš„é›†åˆç±»ï¼Œè¿™äº›é›†åˆç±»ä¹‹é—´æœ‰ç›¸åŒçš„å±æ€§æˆ–è€…è¡Œä¸ºï¼Œé›†åˆä¸é›†åˆä¹‹é—´ä¼šå½¢æˆç»§æ‰¿ä½“ç³»ã€‚

#### é›†åˆçš„ç»§æ‰¿ä½“ç³»

#### é›†åˆCollectionçˆ¶æ¥å£

##### 1ã€æ¦‚è¿°

> ```
> é€šè¿‡è§‚å¯Ÿå‘ç°Collectionæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªæ¥å£ï¼Œå…¶ä¸­åªæœ‰æŠ½è±¡æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œæ¥å£æ— æ³•å®ä¾‹åŒ–ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥æˆ‘ä»¬è¦æ‰¾è¯¥æ¥å£çš„å®ç°å­ç±»ï¼Œå€ŸåŠ©è¿™ä¸ªå­ç±»å­¦ä¹ ä½¿ç”¨Collectionä¸­çš„æ–¹æ³•
> Collectionä¸‹é¢åˆæœ‰ä¸¤å¤§å­æ¥å£
>     - Listæ¥å£
>         - å®ç°å­ç±»ï¼šArrayList
>     - Setæ¥å£
> ```

##### 2ã€é€šè¿‡ARRayListå®ç°Collectionä¸­çš„æ–¹æ³•

> ```
>  ArrayListæ˜¯å®ç°äº†Listæ¥å£çš„å…·ä½“å­ç±»ï¼ŒListæ¥å£æ˜¯ç»§æ‰¿è‡ªCollectionæ¥å£
>    å€ŸåŠ©åˆ›å»ºArrayListå¯¹è±¡ï¼Œæ¥ä½¿ç”¨å­¦ä¹ Collectionæ¥å£ä¸­çš„æ–¹æ³•
> 
>    ArrayListç±»ä¸­æœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªæ— å‚æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œå¯ä»¥è®©æˆ‘ä»¬åˆ›å»ºä¸€ä¸ªç©ºçš„é›†åˆ
> 
>    Collectionä¸­çš„æŠ½è±¡æ–¹æ³•ä¸€å®šä¼šåœ¨å…·ä½“å­ç±»ArrayListä¸­æ‰¾åˆ°å®ç°ï¼š
>        boolean add(Object e)
>        boolean remove(Object o)
>        void clear()
>        boolean contains(Object o)
>        boolean isEmpty()
>        int size()
> 
>    æ³¨æ„ï¼š
>        1ã€javaä¸­çš„é›†åˆåªèƒ½å­˜å‚¨å¼•ç”¨æ•°æ®ç±»å‹
>        2ã€
> 
> */
> ```

~~~java
package com.shujia.day11;

import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.ArrayList;
public class CollectionDemo2 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Collection c1 = new ArrayList();

        //boolean add(Object e) å‘é›†åˆä¸­æ·»åŠ å…ƒç´  å¯ä»¥å­˜æ”¾ä»»æ„çš„å¼•ç”¨æ•°æ®ç±»å‹
        c1.add(10); // è¿™é‡Œåº•å±‚æ¶‰åŠåˆ°ä»Šå¤©è¯´çš„è‡ªåŠ¨è£…ç®± int:10 --> Integer
        /*
            ArrayList extends AbstractList
            AbstractList extends AbstractCollection
         */
        c1.add(12.34);
        c1.add("hello");
        c1.add(true);
        c1.add(true);
        System.out.println("c1: " + c1); // c1: [10] // toString()åº•å±‚å®é™…ä½¿ç”¨çš„æ˜¯ArrayListçš„çˆ¶ç±»çš„çˆ¶ç±»AbstractCollectionä¸­çš„toString()

        System.out.println("-------------------[");
        //boolean remove(Object o)
        c1.remove(true); // è°ƒç”¨ä¸€æ¬¡ï¼Œåªä¼šåˆ ä¸€æ¬¡å€¼
        System.out.println("c1: " + c1);
        System.out.println("-------------------[");
        //void clear() æ¸…ç©ºé›†åˆ
//        c1.clear();
//        System.out.println("c1: " + c1);
        System.out.println("-------------------[");
        //boolean contains(Object o) åˆ¤æ–­é›†åˆæ˜¯å¦åŒ…å«æŸä¸ªå…ƒç´ 
        System.out.println(c1.contains(43));
        System.out.println("-------------------[");
        //boolean isEmpty()
        System.out.println(c1.isEmpty());
        System.out.println("-------------------[");
        //int size() è·å–é›†åˆä¸­çš„å…ƒç´ ä¸ªæ•°
        System.out.println(c1.size());

    }
}

~~~

###### 2.1Collectionä¸­çš„æ–¹æ³•

~~~Java
package com.shujia.day11;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collection;

/*
    Collectionä¸­çš„æ–¹æ³•ï¼š
        boolean addAll(Collection c)
        boolean removeAll(Collection c)
        boolean containsAll(Collection c)
        boolean retainAll(Collection c)

 */
public class CollectionDemo3 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Collection c1 = new ArrayList();
        c1.add("java");
        c1.add("maven&git");
        c1.add("redis");
        c1.add("clickhouse");
        c1.add("hadoop");
        System.out.println("c1: " + c1);

        Collection c2 = new ArrayList();
        c2.add("redis");
        c2.add("clickhouse");
        c2.add("hadoop");
        c2.add("hive");
        System.out.println("c2: " + c2);
~~~

###### 3.1ã€å­˜å‚¨è‡ªå®šä¹‰å¯¹è±¡å¹¶éå†

~~~Java
package com.shujia.day12;

public class Student {
    private String name;
    private int age;

    public Student() {
    }

    public Student(String name, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }

    public String getName() {
        return name;
    }

    public void setName(String name) {
        this.name = name;
    }

    public int getAge() {
        return age;
    }

    public void setAge(int age) {
        this.age = age;
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return "Student{" +
                "name='" + name + '\'' +
                ", age=" + age +
                '}';
    }
}
~~~



~~~Java
package com.shujia.day12;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.Iterator;

/*
    å­˜å‚¨è‡ªå®šä¹‰å¯¹è±¡å¹¶éå†
        Student(name,age)

 */
public class CollectionDemo1 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        //1ã€åˆ›å»ºé›†åˆå¯¹è±¡
        Collection c1 = new ArrayList();

        //2ã€åˆ›å»ºå…ƒç´ å¯¹è±¡
        Student s1 = new Student("å¼ ä¸‰", 12);
        Student s2 = new Student("æå››", 14);
        Student s3 = new Student("ç‹äº”", 12);
        Student s4 = new Student("èµµå…­", 13);

        //3ã€å°†å…ƒç´ æ·»åŠ åˆ°é›†åˆä¸­
        c1.add(s1);
        c1.add(s2);
        c1.add(s3);
        c1.add(s4);

        //4ã€éå†é›†åˆ
        //4.1å…ˆè½¬æ•°ç»„éå†
//        Object[] objects = c1.toArray();
//        for (int i = 0; i < objects.length; i++) {
//            Student student = (Student) objects[i];
//            System.out.println(student.getName() + "--" + student.getAge());
//        }

        //4.2è¿­ä»£å™¨éå†
        Iterator iterator = c1.iterator(); // new Itr()
        while (iterator.hasNext()) {
            Student student = (Student) iterator.next();
            System.out.println(student.getName() + "--" + student.getAge());
        }


    }
}
~~~

~~~java
 å› ä¸ºListç›¸å…³é›†åˆå…·å¤‡äº†ç´¢å¼•çš„æ¦‚å¿µï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥Listé›†åˆå®ƒé‡Œé¢å°±ä¼šå‡ºç°ä¸ç´¢å¼•ç›¸å…³çš„æ–¹æ³•

     public class ListDemo2 {

        //[java, mysql, hadoop, hive, apple]

        System.out.println("================================");

        Object o1 = list1.set(4, "datax"); //é€šè¿‡ç´¢å¼•è®¾ç½®å…ƒç´ å€¼ï¼Œè¿”å›åŸå§‹çš„å…ƒç´ 
        System.out.println(o1);
        System.out.println("list1: " + list1);
        System.out.println("================================");

        ListIterator listIterator = list1.listIterator();
        while (listIterator.hasNext()){
            System.out.println(listIterator.next());
        }
        System.out.println("--------------");
        //æ— è®ºæ˜¯ListIteratorè¿­ä»£å™¨ï¼Œè¿˜æ˜¯Iteratorè¿­ä»£å™¨ï¼ŒæŒ‡é’ˆåªæœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªï¼Œè€Œä¸”æœ€å¼€å§‹çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œåœ¨è¿­ä»£å™¨çš„æœ€å·¦è¾¹
        //æ‰€ä»¥è¦æƒ³åå‘éå†ï¼Œå¾—å…ˆæ­£å‘éå†ä¸€éï¼Œå°†æŒ‡é’ˆç§»åŠ¨åˆ°æœ€å³è¾¹ï¼Œ
        while (listIterator.hasPrevious()){
            System.out.println(listIterator.previous());
        }


    }
~~~

##### 3ã€æ¡ˆä¾‹

###### 3.1ã€ä½¿ç”¨ArrayListå»é™¤é›†åˆä¸­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²çš„é‡å¤å€¼(å­—ç¬¦ä¸²çš„å†…å®¹ç›¸åŒ)

~~~Java
public class ArrayListTest1 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        //åˆ›å»ºé›†åˆå¯¹è±¡
        ArrayList list1 = new ArrayList();

        //æ·»åŠ ä¸€äº›å­—ç¬¦ä¸²
        list1.add("java");
        list1.add("hadoop");
        list1.add("hive");
        list1.add("hbase");
        list1.add("æ•°æ®é‡‡é›†");
        list1.add("hive");
        list1.add("hadoop");
        list1.add("hive");

        //åˆ›å»ºä¸€ä¸ªæ–°ç©ºé›†åˆ
        ArrayList list2 = new ArrayList();

        //éå†æ—§é›†åˆï¼Œåˆ¤æ–­æ–°é›†åˆä¸­æ˜¯å¦å­˜åœ¨è¯¥å…ƒç´ ï¼Œå¦‚æœæœ‰ï¼Œè¯´æ˜é‡å¤ï¼Œå°±ä¸æ·»åŠ åˆ°æ–°é›†åˆä¸­ï¼Œå¦åˆ™å°±æ·»åŠ 
        Iterator iterator = list1.iterator();
        while (iterator.hasNext()) {
            String s = (String) iterator.next();
            if (!list2.contains(s)) {
                list2.add(s);
            }
        }

        System.out.println("list1: " + list1);
        System.out.println("list2: " + list2);


    }
}
~~~

###### 3.2ã€ä½¿ç”¨ArrayListå»é™¤é›†åˆä¸­è‡ªå®šä¹‰å¯¹è±¡çš„é‡å¤å€¼(å¯¹è±¡çš„æˆå‘˜å˜é‡å€¼éƒ½ç›¸åŒ)

~~~Java
package com.shujia.day12;

import java.util.Objects;

public class Teacher {
    private String name;
    private int age;

    public Teacher() {
    }

    public Teacher(String name, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }

    public String getName() {
        return name;
    }

    public void setName(String name) {
        this.name = name;
    }

    public int getAge() {
        return age;
    }

    public void setAge(int age) {
        this.age = age;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean equals(Object o) {
        if (this == o) return true;
        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) return false;
        Teacher teacher = (Teacher) o;
        return age == teacher.age && Objects.equals(name, teacher.name);
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return "Teacher{" +
                "name='" + name + '\'' +
                ", age=" + age +
                '}';
    }
}
~~~



~~~Java
package com.shujia.day12;

/*
    ä½¿ç”¨ArrayListå»é™¤é›†åˆä¸­è‡ªå®šä¹‰å¯¹è±¡çš„é‡å¤å€¼(å¯¹è±¡çš„æˆå‘˜å˜é‡å€¼éƒ½ç›¸åŒ)
    æŒ‰ç…§ä¸Šä¸€ä¸ªå»é‡å­—ç¬¦ä¸²çš„é€»è¾‘å¯¹å¯¹è±¡è¿›è¡Œå»é‡å‘ç°ï¼Œå¹¶æ²¡æœ‰å»é‡
    ç»è¿‡ç®€å•çš„åˆ†æåå‘ç°ï¼Œif (!list2.contains(t))æ°¸è¿œä¸ºtrue,å…ƒç´ æ‰ä¼šä¸æ–­çš„å‘æ–°é›†åˆä¸­æ·»åŠ 
    !list2.contains(t)æ•´ä½“æ°¸è¿œä¸ºtrue, æ„å‘³ç€list2.contains(t)æ°¸è¿œä¸ºfalse
    ç°åœ¨åº”è¯¥å»çœ‹contains()æ–¹æ³•çš„æºç 

    public boolean contains(Object o) {
        return indexOf(o) >= 0; //  indexOf(o)æ°¸è¿œä¸º-1  indexOf(o) >= 0 æ°¸è¿œä¸ºfalse
    }

    public int indexOf(Object o) {
        if (o == null) {
            for (int i = 0; i < size; i++)
                if (elementData[i]==null)
                    return i;
        } else {
            for (int i = 0; i < size; i++)
                if (o.equals(elementData[i]))
                    return i;
        }
        return -1;
    }

    é€šè¿‡åˆ†æåå‘ç°ï¼Œåº•å±‚åˆ¤æ–­å…ƒç´ æ˜¯å¦é‡å¤ï¼Œæ˜¯è°ƒç”¨äº†å…ƒç´ ç±»å‹ä¸­çš„equalsæ–¹æ³•æ¥æ¯”è¾ƒçš„ï¼Œè€Œæˆ‘ä»¬Teacherç±»ä¸­æ²¡æœ‰é‡å†™equalsæ–¹æ³•
    è°ƒç”¨çš„æ˜¯çˆ¶äº²Objectç±»ä¸­çš„equalsæ–¹æ³•ï¼Œè€ŒObjectç±»ä¸­çš„equalsæ¯”è¾ƒçš„æ˜¯åœ°å€å€¼ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬çš„æ¯ä¸€ä¸ªTeacherå¯¹è±¡éƒ½æ˜¯newå‡ºæ¥çš„ï¼Œåœ°å€å€¼è‚¯å®šä¸ä¸€æ ·
    æ‰€ä»¥equalsæ¯”è¾ƒçš„ç»“æœæ°¸è¿œä¸ºfalse
    è¦æƒ³è¾¾åˆ°å»é‡æ•ˆæœï¼Œå°±åº”è¯¥æ¯”è¾ƒå¯¹è±¡çš„æˆå‘˜å˜é‡å€¼ï¼Œè€Œä¸æ˜¯æ¯”è¾ƒåœ°å€å€¼ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬åº”è¯¥æ˜¯å½“å¯¹è±¡çš„æˆå‘˜å˜é‡å€¼ç›¸åŒçš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œè®¤ä¸ºæ˜¯åŒä¸€ä¸ªå¯¹è±¡
    åªéœ€è¦å…ƒç´ çš„ç±»å‹ä¸­é‡å†™equalsæ–¹æ³•å³å¯ï¼Œè‡ªåŠ¨ç”Ÿæˆå³å¯ã€‚

 */


import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Iterator;

public class ArrayListTest2 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        //åˆ›å»ºé›†åˆå¯¹è±¡
        ArrayList list = new ArrayList();

        //åˆ›å»ºå…ƒç´ å¯¹è±¡
        Teacher t1 = new Teacher("å°è™", 18);
        Teacher t2 = new Teacher("é˜¿å½ª", 17);
        Teacher t3 = new Teacher("é˜¿å‡¤", 15);
        Teacher t4 = new Teacher("å°å®", 17);
        Teacher t5 = new Teacher("å°è™", 18);

        //å°†å…ƒç´ æ·»åŠ åˆ°é›†åˆä¸­
        list.add(t1);
        list.add(t2);
        list.add(t3);
        list.add(t4);
        list.add(t5);

        //åˆ›å»ºä¸€ä¸ªæ–°ç©ºé›†åˆ
        ArrayList list2 = new ArrayList();

        //éå†æ—§é›†åˆï¼Œåˆ¤æ–­æ–°é›†åˆä¸­æ˜¯å¦å­˜åœ¨è¯¥å…ƒç´ ï¼Œå¦‚æœæœ‰ï¼Œè¯´æ˜é‡å¤ï¼Œå°±ä¸æ·»åŠ åˆ°æ–°é›†åˆä¸­ï¼Œå¦åˆ™å°±æ·»åŠ 
        Iterator iterator = list.iterator();
        while (iterator.hasNext()) {
            Teacher t = (Teacher) iterator.next();
            if (!list2.contains(t)) {
                list2.add(t);
            }
        }

        System.out.println("list1: " + list);
        System.out.println("list2: " + list2);
    }
}
~~~

~~~Java
public class LinkedListDemo1 {
~~~

##### 3ã€æ¡ˆä¾‹

> ```java
> è¯·ç”¨LinkedListæ¨¡æ‹Ÿæ ˆæ•°æ®ç»“æ„çš„é›†åˆï¼Œå¹¶æµ‹è¯•

~~~java
package com.shujia.day12;

import java.util.LinkedList;

public class MyStack {
    private LinkedList linkedList;

    public MyStack() {
        linkedList = new LinkedList();
    }

    public void myAdd(Object obj){
        linkedList.addFirst(obj);
    }

    public Object myGet(){
        return linkedList.removeFirst();
    }

    public int getLength(){
        return linkedList.size();
    }


}
~~~


###### 3.3ã€æ³›å‹æ¥å£

> ```java
> å¦‚æœä¸€ä¸ªç±»å®ç°ä¸€ä¸ªæ¥å£ï¼Œè¿™ä¸ªæ¥å£æœ‰æ³›å‹çš„è¯ï¼Œç±»å®šä¹‰æ—¶ï¼Œä¹Ÿè¦æœ‰æ³›å‹ï¼Œä¸€èˆ¬æƒ…å†µä¸‹ä¸æ¥å£çš„æ³›å‹å†™æ³•ä¸€è‡´

~~~java
interface Inter1<E>{
    void fun1(E e);
}

//å¦‚æœä¸€ä¸ªç±»å®ç°ä¸€ä¸ªæ¥å£ï¼Œè¿™ä¸ªæ¥å£æœ‰æ³›å‹çš„è¯ï¼Œç±»å®šä¹‰æ—¶ï¼Œä¹Ÿè¦æœ‰æ³›å‹ï¼Œä¸€èˆ¬æƒ…å†µä¸‹ä¸æ¥å£çš„æ³›å‹å†™æ³•ä¸€è‡´
class Demo3<E> implements Inter1<E>{
    @Override
    public void fun1(E e) {
        System.out.println(e);
    }
}

/*
    æ³›å‹æ¥å£ï¼šå°†æ³›å‹å®šä¹‰åœ¨æ¥å£ä¸Š
 */
public class FanXingDemo3 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Inter1<String> s = new Demo3<>();
        s.fun1("abc");

        /*
                interface List<E>
                class ArrayList<E> implements List<E>{
                    add(E e){}
                }
         */
        List<String> list = new ArrayList<>();
        list.add("dsa");
//        list.add(12);

    }
}
~~~

~~~Java
public class KeBianCanShuDemo {

        //éœ€æ±‚1ï¼šå®šä¹‰ä¸€ä¸ªæ–¹æ³•ï¼Œæ±‚ä¸¤ä¸ªintç±»å‹å€¼çš„å’Œ

    public static String sumScore(String name, int... scores) {
        int sumNum = 0;
        for (int i : scores) {
            sumNum += i;
        }
        return "å§“åï¼š"+name+", æ€»åˆ†ï¼š"+sumNum;
    }

        }
        return sumNum;
~~~

~~~Java
        ArrayList<String> list1 = new ArrayList<>();
        ArrayList<Integer> list2 = new ArrayList<>();
        ArrayList<Student> list3 = new ArrayList<>();
        list3.add(new Student("å¼ ä¸‰",18));
        list3.add(new Student("æå››",19));
        list2.add(15);
        list2.add(33);
        list2.add(55);
        list1.add("java");
        list1.add("hbase");
        list1.add("hadoop");
        list1.add("hive");

        list.add(list1);
        list.add(list2);
        list.add(list3);
~~~

~~~Java
public class ListTest2 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Random random = new Random();
        ArrayList<Integer> list = new ArrayList<>();
        int size = 0;
        while (size<=10){
            int number = random.nextInt(20)+1;
            if(!list.contains(number)){
                list.add(number);
            }
            size=list.size();
        }

        System.out.println(list);
    }

}
~~~

~~~Java
public class ListTest3 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
        ArrayList<Integer> list = new ArrayList<>();
        while (true){
            System.out.println("è¾“å…¥ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°æ®ï¼š");
            int number = sc.nextInt();
            list.add(number);
            if (number==0){
                break;
            }
        }
        Integer maxNumber = list.get(0);

        for (Integer number : list) {
            if (number>maxNumber){
                maxNumber=number;
            }

        }
~~~

##### 4ã€HashSetå¦‚ä½•åšåˆ°å»é‡çš„

###### 4.1ã€HashSetä¸­çš„addæ–¹æ³•çš„æºç è§£é‡Š

~~~Java

public class HashSet<E> implements Set<E>{
    private transient HashMap<E,Object> map;
    private static final Object PRESENT = new Object();

    public HashSet() {
        map = new HashMap<>();
    }

    //set1.add("pitaya");
    public boolean add(E e) {
        //HashSetä¸­çš„addæ–¹æ³•åº•å±‚æ˜¯è°ƒç”¨äº†HashMapä¸­çš„putæ–¹æ³•
        // e -- "pitaya"
        // PRESENT -- new Object()
        return map.put(e, PRESENT)==null;
    }
}


public class HashMap<K,V> implements Map<K,V>{
    public HashMap() {
        this.loadFactor = DEFAULT_LOAD_FACTOR; // all other fields defaulted
    }

    static final int hash(Object key) {
        int h;
        return (key == null) ? 0 : (h = key.hashCode()) ^ (h >>> 16);
    }

    public V put(K key, V value) {
        // key -- "pitaya"
        // value -- new Object()
        // ä¸å…ƒç´ ç±»å‹ä¸­çš„hashCodeæ–¹æ³•æœ‰å…³
        return putVal(hash(key), key, value, false, true);
    }

    final V putVal(int hash, K key, V value, boolean onlyIfAbsent,boolean evict) {
        Node<K,V>[] tab;
        Node<K,V> p;
        int n, i;
        //ç¬¬ä¸€æ¬¡åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸€ä¸ªhashTableå‡ºæ¥
        if ((tab = table) == null || (n = tab.length) == 0)
            n = (tab = resize()).length;
        //ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå…ƒç´ ï¼Œç›´æ¥æ”¾å…¥åˆ°å“ˆå¸Œè¡¨ä¸­
        if ((p = tab[i = (n - 1) & hash]) == null)
            tab[i] = newNode(hash, key, value, null);
        else {
            Node<K,V> e;
            K k;
            //åˆ¤æ–­å¾…æ’å…¥çš„å…ƒç´ ä¸å·²ç»åœ¨å“ˆå¸Œè¡¨ä¸­çš„å…ƒç´ 
            //1ã€å“ˆå¸Œå€¼æ˜¯å¦ä¸€æ · å…ƒç´ ç±».hashCode()æ–¹æ³•
            //2ã€å†…å®¹å€¼æ˜¯å¦ä¸€æ · å…ƒç´ ç±».equals()æ–¹æ³•
            if (p.hash == hash && ((k = p.key) == key || (key != null && key.equals(k))))
                e = p;
            else if (p instanceof TreeNode)
                e = ((TreeNode<K,V>)p).putTreeVal(this, tab, hash, key, value);
            else {
                for (int binCount = 0; ; ++binCount) {
                    if ((e = p.next) == null) {
                        p.next = newNode(hash, key, value, null);
                        if (binCount >= TREEIFY_THRESHOLD - 1) // -1 for 1st
                            treeifyBin(tab, hash);
                        break;
                    }
                    if (e.hash == hash &&
                        ((k = e.key) == key || (key != null && key.equals(k))))
                        break;
                    p = e;
                }
            }
            if (e != null) { // existing mapping for key
                V oldValue = e.value;
                if (!onlyIfAbsent || oldValue == null)
                    e.value = value;
                afterNodeAccess(e);
                return oldValue;
            }
        }
        ++modCount;
        if (++size > threshold)
            resize();
        afterNodeInsertion(evict);
        return null;
    }

}
~~~

###### 4.2ã€ä¸¾ä¾‹

~~~Java
package com.shujia.day13;
/*
    ä½¿ç”¨HashSetå­˜å‚¨å­¦ç”Ÿå¯¹è±¡ï¼Œå½“å­¦ç”Ÿå¯¹è±¡çš„å§“åå’Œå¹´é¾„ä¸€æ ·çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œè¡¨ç¤ºæ˜¯åŒä¸€ä¸ªå­¦ç”Ÿï¼Œåº”è¯¥è¦è¿›è¡Œå»é‡

    ç»“è®ºï¼š
        HashSetä¸­è¦æƒ³ä¿è¯å…ƒç´ å”¯ä¸€ï¼Œå°±è¦ä¿è¯å…ƒç´ ç±»ä¸­è¦é‡å†™equalså’ŒhashCodeæ–¹æ³•ã€‚

 */

import java.util.HashSet;
import java.util.Objects;

class Student1{
    String name;
    int age;

    public Student1() {
    }

    public Student1(String name, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean equals(Object o) {
        if (this == o) return true;
        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) return false;
        Student1 student1 = (Student1) o;
        return age == student1.age && Objects.equals(name, student1.name);
    }

    @Override
    public int hashCode() {
        return Objects.hash(name, age);
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return "Student1{" +
                "name='" + name + '\'' +
                ", age=" + age +
                '}';
    }
}

public class HashSetDemo1 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        //åˆ›å»ºé›†åˆå¯¹è±¡
        HashSet<Student1> set = new HashSet<>();

        //åˆ›å»ºå…ƒç´ å¯¹è±¡
        Student1 s1 = new Student1("å°šå¹³", 18);
        Student1 s2 = new Student1("ä¸ä¹‰æ°", 16);
        Student1 s3 = new Student1("é»„æ°", 18);
        Student1 s4 = new Student1("å°šå¹³", 18);
        Student1 s5 = new Student1("æ±ªæƒ", 17);

        //å°†å…ƒç´ æ·»åŠ åˆ°é›†åˆä¸­
        set.add(s1);
        set.add(s2);
        set.add(s3);
        set.add(s4);
        set.add(s5);

        //éå†é›†åˆ
        for (Student1 s : set) {
            System.out.println(s);
        }

    }
}
~~~

#### Setæ¥å£-TreeSetç±»

##### 1ã€TreeSetç±»æ¦‚è¿°

> ä½¿ç”¨å…ƒç´ çš„è‡ªç„¶é¡ºåºå¯¹å…ƒç´ è¿›è¡Œæ’åº
> æˆ–è€…æ ¹æ®åˆ›å»º set æ—¶æä¾›çš„ Comparator è¿›è¡Œæ’åº
> å…·ä½“å–å†³äºä½¿ç”¨çš„æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•ã€‚ 

##### 2ã€ä¸¾ä¾‹

~~~Java
package com.shujia.day13;

import java.util.TreeSet;

/*
    Collection
        - List
            -- ArrayList
            -- Vector
            -- LinkedList
        - Set(æ¥å£) å…ƒç´ æ— åºä¸”å”¯ä¸€
            -- HashSet åº•å±‚æ•°æ®ç»“æ„æ˜¯å“ˆå¸Œè¡¨ï¼Œçº¿ç¨‹ä¸å®‰å…¨çš„ï¼Œæ•ˆç‡é«˜
                --å­ç±»ï¼šLinkedHashSet åº•å±‚æ•°æ®ç»“æ„æ˜¯å“ˆå¸Œè¡¨ä¸åŒå‘é“¾è¡¨
            -- TreeSet åº•å±‚æ•°æ®ç»“æ„æ˜¯çº¢é»‘æ ‘ï¼ˆå¯æ’åºçš„ï¼‰ï¼Œçº¿ç¨‹ä¸å®‰å…¨ï¼Œæ•ˆç‡é«˜

    TreeSetä¸­çš„æ’åºæ–¹å¼æœ‰ä¸¤ç§ï¼š
        1ã€è‡ªç„¶æ’åº  Comparable
        2ã€æ¯”è¾ƒå™¨æ’åº comparator
    éœ€æ±‚1ï¼šä½¿ç”¨TreeSetå­˜å‚¨å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å¯¹è±¡ï¼Œå¹¶éå†

    é€šè¿‡è§‚å¯Ÿæºç å‘ç°ï¼Œå› ä¸ºæˆ‘ä»¬åˆ›å»ºTreeSeté›†åˆå¯¹è±¡çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨çš„æ˜¯æ— å‚æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•
    æ‰€ä»¥åº•å±‚åˆ›å»ºTreeMapçš„æ—¶å€™ä¹Ÿæ˜¯æ— å‚æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œcomparatoræ˜¯nullï¼Œä¸èµ°æ¯”è¾ƒå™¨æ’åº
    èµ°çš„æ˜¯è‡ªç„¶æ’åº


 */
public class TreeSetDemo1 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        //TreeSet() æ„é€ ä¸€ä¸ªæ–°çš„ï¼Œç©ºçš„æ ‘ç»„ï¼Œæ ¹æ®å…¶å…ƒç´ çš„è‡ªç„¶æ’åºè¿›è¡Œæ’åºã€‚
        //åˆ›å»ºä¸€ä¸ªç©ºçš„TreeSeté›†åˆå¯¹è±¡
        TreeSet<String> treeSet = new TreeSet<>();

        //åˆ›å»ºå…ƒç´ å¯¹è±¡å¹¶æ·»åŠ åˆ°é›†åˆä¸­
        treeSet.add("java");
        treeSet.add("hadoop");
        treeSet.add("redis");
        treeSet.add("clickhouse");
        treeSet.add("hbase");
        treeSet.add("java");

        //éå†é›†åˆ
        for (String s : treeSet) {
            System.out.println(s);
        }

    }
}
~~~

##### 3ã€TreeSetå¦‚ä½•è¿›è¡Œæ’åºçš„

###### 3.1ã€TreeSetä¸­çš„addæ–¹æ³•çš„æºç è§£é‡Š

~~~Java
public class TreeSet<E>{
    private transient NavigableMap<E,Object> m;
    private static final Object PRESENT = new Object();

    public TreeSet() {
        this(new TreeMap<E,Object>()); // this(..)
    }

    public TreeSet(Comparator<? super E> comparator) {
        this(new TreeMap<>(comparator));
    }

    TreeSet(NavigableMap<E,Object> m) {
        this.m = m;
    }

    // treeSet.add(s2);
    public boolean add(E e) {
        //TreeSetä¸­addæ–¹æ³•åº•å±‚è°ƒç”¨çš„æ˜¯TreeMapä¸­çš„putæ–¹æ³•
        //e -- s2
        //PRESENT -- new Object()
        return m.put(e, PRESENT)==null;
    }
}


public class TreeMap{
    private final Comparator<? super K> comparator;
    private transient Entry<K,V> root;

    public TreeMap() {
        comparator = null;
    }

    public TreeMap(Comparator<? super K> comparator) {
        this.comparator = comparator;
    }

    public V put(K key, V value) {
        // key -- "hadoop"
        // value -- new Object()
        Entry<K,V> t = root; // null
        //å¦‚æœè¯´æ˜¯ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå…ƒç´ æ’å…¥è¿›æ¥ï¼Œè¿™ä¸ªå…ƒç´ å°±ä½œä¸ºçº¢é»‘æ ‘çš„æ ¹ä¿å­˜
        if (t == null) {
            compare(key, key); // type (and possibly null) check

            root = new Entry<>(key, value, null); // s1
            size = 1;
            modCount++;
            return null;
        }
        int cmp;
        Entry<K,V> parent;
        // split comparator and comparable paths
        Comparator<? super K> cpr = comparator; // null
        //æ¯”è¾ƒå™¨æ’åº
        if (cpr != null) {
            do {
                parent = t;
                cmp = cpr.compare(key, t.key);
                if (cmp < 0)
                    t = t.left;
                else if (cmp > 0)
                    t = t.right;
                else
                    return t.setValue(value);
            } while (t != null);
        }
        //è‡ªç„¶æ’åº
        else {
            if (key == null) // s2
                throw new NullPointerException();
            @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
                Comparable<? super K> k = (Comparable<? super K>) key;
            do {
                parent = t; // "java"
                cmp = k.compareTo(t.key); // 1
                if (cmp < 0)
                    t = t.left;
                else if (cmp > 0)
                    t = t.right;
                else
                    return t.setValue(value);
            } while (t != null);
        }
        Entry<K,V> e = new Entry<>(key, value, parent);
        if (cmp < 0)
            parent.left = e;
        else
            parent.right = e;
        fixAfterInsertion(e);
        size++;
        modCount++;
        return null;
    }



}
~~~

###### 3.2ã€ä¸¾ä¾‹1-è‡ªç„¶æ’åº

~~~Java
package com.shujia.day13;

import java.util.TreeSet;

/*
    ä½¿ç”¨TreeSeté›†åˆå­˜å‚¨è‡ªå®šä¹‰å¯¹è±¡Student2(String name,int age)
    è¦æ±‚ï¼šæœ€ç»ˆè¦æŒ‰ç…§å¹´é¾„ä»å°åˆ°å¤§æ’åºï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”å½“å­¦ç”Ÿçš„å§“åå’Œå¹´é¾„ä¸€æ ·çš„æ—¶å€™è¦è¿›è¡Œå»é‡

    æˆ‘ä»¬æŒ‰ç…§å­˜å‚¨å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸€æ ·çš„é€»è¾‘å­˜å‚¨è‡ªå®šä¹‰å¯¹è±¡ï¼Œè¿è¡Œçš„æ—¶å€™æŠ¥é”™äº†
    ClassCastExceptionï¼š
    com.shujia.day13.Student2 cannot be cast to java.lang.Comparable
    åŸå› æ˜¯å› ä¸ºï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬ç°åœ¨ä½¿ç”¨çš„æ—¶å€™è‡ªç„¶æ’åºæ–¹å¼ï¼Œéœ€è¦å…ƒç´ çš„ç±»å®ç°Comparableæ¥å£ï¼Œæ‰å¯ä»¥è¿›è¡Œè½¬å‹

 */
class Student2 implements Comparable<Student2> {
    String name;
    int age;

    public Student2() {
    }

    public Student2(String name, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return "Student{" +
                "name='" + name + '\'' +
                ", age=" + age +
                '}';
    }

    @Override
    public int compareTo(Student2 s) {
//        return 0;
//        return -1;
//        return 1;
        //æ˜¾å¼æ¡ä»¶ï¼šæŒ‰ç…§å¹´é¾„ä»å°åˆ°å¤§æ’åº
        //this -- å¾…æ’å…¥çš„å…ƒç´ 
        //o -- å·²ç»åœ¨æ ‘ä¸­çš„æ ¹
//        return  this.age-s.age;
        //éšè—æ¡ä»¶ï¼šå½“å¹´é¾„ä¸€æ ·çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œæ¯”è¾ƒå§“å
        int i1 = this.age - s.age;
        return (i1 == 0) ? this.name.compareTo(s.name) : i1;
    }
}

public class TreeSetDemo2 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        //åˆ›å»ºé›†åˆå¯¹è±¡
        TreeSet<Student2> treeSet = new TreeSet<>();

        //åˆ›å»ºå…ƒç´ å¯¹è±¡
        //ç»ˆè¦æŒ‰ç…§å¹´é¾„ä»å°åˆ°å¤§æ’åº
        Student2 s1 = new Student2("å¼ ä¸‰", 16);
        Student2 s2 = new Student2("æå››", 16);
        Student2 s3 = new Student2("ç‹äº”", 15);
        Student2 s4 = new Student2("èµµå…­", 12);
        Student2 s5 = new Student2("å¼ ä¸‰", 16);

        //å°†å­¦ç”Ÿå¯¹è±¡æ·»åŠ åˆ°é›†åˆä¸­
        treeSet.add(s1);
        treeSet.add(s2);
        treeSet.add(s3);
        treeSet.add(s4);
        treeSet.add(s5);

        //éå†é›†åˆ
        for (Student2 student2 : treeSet) {
            System.out.println(student2);
        }
    }
}
~~~

###### 3.3 ä¸¾ä¾‹2-æ¯”è¾ƒå™¨æ’åº

~~~Java
package com.shujia.day13;

import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.TreeSet;

/*
    æ¯”è¾ƒå™¨æ’åºï¼š
        public TreeSet(Comparator<? super E> comparator) {
            this(new TreeMap<>(comparator));
        }

    å°æ€»ç»“ï¼š
        1ã€å¦‚æœè¦ä½¿ç”¨è‡ªç„¶æ’åºï¼Œåœ¨åˆ›å»ºTreeSetå¯¹è±¡çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨æ— å‚æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œ
            ä½†æ˜¯è¦ä¿è¯å…ƒç´ çš„ç±»å®ç°Comparableæ¥å£ï¼Œé‡å†™compareToæ–¹æ³•ã€‚
        2ã€å¦‚æœè¦ä½¿ç”¨æ¯”è¾ƒå™¨æ’åºï¼Œåœ¨åˆ›å»ºTreeSetå¯¹è±¡çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨æœ‰å‚æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œ
            ä¼ å…¥ä¸€ä¸ªå®ç°äº†Comparatoræ¥å£çš„å­ç±»å¯¹è±¡ï¼Œé‡å†™compareæ–¹æ³•
 */
class Student3 {
    String name;
    int age;

    public Student3() {
    }

    public Student3(String name, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return "Student{" +
                "name='" + name + '\'' +
                ", age=" + age +
                '}';
    }
}

public class TreeSetDemo3 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        //åˆ›å»ºé›†åˆå¯¹è±¡
        TreeSet<Student3> treeSet = new TreeSet<>(new Comparator<Student3>() {
            @Override
            public int compare(Student3 o1, Student3 o2) {
                //o1 -- å¾…æ’å…¥çš„å…ƒç´ 
                //o2 -- å·²ç»å­˜åœ¨æ ‘ä¸­çš„æ ¹
                int i1 = o1.age - o2.age;
                return (i1 == 0) ? o1.name.compareTo(o2.name) : i1;
            }
        });

        //åˆ›å»ºå…ƒç´ å¯¹è±¡
        //ç»ˆè¦æŒ‰ç…§å¹´é¾„ä»å°åˆ°å¤§æ’åº
        Student3 s1 = new Student3("å¼ ä¸‰", 16);
        Student3 s2 = new Student3("æå››", 16);
        Student3 s3 = new Student3("ç‹äº”", 15);
        Student3 s4 = new Student3("èµµå…­", 12);
        Student3 s5 = new Student3("å¼ ä¸‰", 16);

        //å°†å­¦ç”Ÿå¯¹è±¡æ·»åŠ åˆ°é›†åˆä¸­
        treeSet.add(s1);
        treeSet.add(s2);
        treeSet.add(s3);
        treeSet.add(s4);
        treeSet.add(s5);

        //éå†é›†åˆ
        for (Student3 student3 : treeSet) {
            System.out.println(student3);
        }
    }
}
~~~

#### Seté›†åˆç»ƒä¹ 

##### 1ã€ç¼–å†™ä¸€ä¸ªç¨‹åºï¼Œè·å–10ä¸ª1è‡³20çš„éšæœºæ•°ï¼Œè¦æ±‚éšæœºæ•°ä¸èƒ½é‡å¤ã€‚

~~~Java
package lianxi.day13;


/*
ç¼–å†™ä¸€ä¸ªç¨‹åºï¼Œè·å–10ä¸ª1è‡³20çš„éšæœºæ•°ï¼Œè¦æ±‚éšæœºæ•°ä¸èƒ½é‡å¤ã€‚

 */

import java.util.Random;
import java.util.TreeSet;

public class TreeSetTest1 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        TreeSet<Integer> treeSet = new TreeSet<>();
        Random random = new Random();
        while (true){
            int number = random.nextInt(20)+1;
            treeSet.add(number);
            if (treeSet.size()==10){
                break;
            }
        }
        System.out.println(treeSet);
    }
}
~~~

##### 2ã€é”®ç›˜å½•å…¥5ä¸ªå­¦ç”Ÿä¿¡æ¯(å§“å,è¯­æ–‡æˆç»©,æ•°å­¦æˆç»©,è‹±è¯­æˆç»©),æŒ‰ç…§æ€»åˆ†ä»é«˜åˆ°ä½è¾“å‡ºåˆ°æ§åˆ¶å°

~~~Java
package lianxi.day13;

import java.util.Scanner;

/*
é”®ç›˜å½•å…¥5ä¸ªå­¦ç”Ÿä¿¡æ¯(å§“å,è¯­æ–‡æˆç»©,æ•°å­¦æˆç»©,è‹±è¯­æˆç»©),æŒ‰ç…§æ€»åˆ†ä»é«˜åˆ°ä½è¾“å‡ºåˆ°æ§åˆ¶å°

 */

import java.util.TreeSet;

class Student3 implements Comparable {
    private String name;
    private int chineseScore;
    private int mathScore;
    private int englishScore;
    private int sumScore;

    public Student3() {
    }

    public Student3(String name, int chineseScore, int mathScore, int englishScore, int sumScore) {
        this.name = name;
        this.chineseScore = chineseScore;
        this.mathScore = mathScore;
        this.englishScore = englishScore;
        this.sumScore = sumScore;
    }

    public String getName() {
        return name;
    }

    public void setName(String name) {
        this.name = name;
    }

    public int getChineseScore() {
        return chineseScore;
    }

    public void setChineseScore(int chineseScore) {
        this.chineseScore = chineseScore;
    }

    public int getMathScore() {
        return mathScore;
    }

    public void setMathScore(int mathScore) {
        this.mathScore = mathScore;
    }

    public int getEnglishScore() {
        return englishScore;
    }

    public void setEnglishScore(int englishScore) {
        this.englishScore = englishScore;
    }
    public void setSumScore(int sumScore){
        this.sumScore=sumScore;
    }
    public int getSumScore(){
        return sumScore;
    }
    public int sumScore(int chineseScore, int mathScore, int englishScore) {
        return chineseScore + mathScore + englishScore;
    }

    @Override
    public int compareTo(Object o) {
        Student3 o1 = (Student3) o;
        int i1 = o1.getSumScore() - this.getSumScore();
        //æ€»åˆ†ä¸€æ ·ï¼Œè¯­æ–‡æˆç»©ä¸ä¸€å®šä¸€æ ·ï¼Œ
        int i2 = (i1 == 0) ? o1.getChineseScore() - this.getChineseScore() : i1;
        //æ€»åˆ†ä¸€æ ·ï¼Œè¯­æ–‡æˆç»©ä¸€æ ·ï¼Œæ•°å­¦æˆç»©ä¸ä¸€å®šä¸€æ ·
        int i3 = (i2 == 0) ? o1.getMathScore() - this.getMathScore() : i2;
        //åˆ†æ•°éƒ½ä¸€æ ·ï¼Œå§“åä¸ä¸€å®šä¸€æ ·
        return (i3 == 0) ? o1.getName().compareTo(this.getName()) : i3;
    }



    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return "Student3{" +
                "name='" + name + '\'' +
                ", chineseScore=" + chineseScore +
                ", mathScore=" + mathScore +
                ", englishScore=" + englishScore +
                ", sumScore=" + sumScore +
                '}';
    }
}

public class TreeSetTest2 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
        TreeSet<Student3> treeSet = new TreeSet<>();
        Student3 s1 = new Student3();
        for (int i = 1; i <= 5; i++) {
            System.out.println("ç¬¬" + i + "å­¦ç”Ÿ");
            System.out.print("å§“å:");
            String name = sc.next();
            System.out.print("è¯­æ–‡æˆç»©:");
            int chineseScore = sc.nextInt();
            System.out.print("æ•°å­¦æˆç»©:");
            int mathScore = sc.nextInt();
            System.out.print("è‹±è¯­æˆç»©:");
            int englishScore = sc.nextInt();
            Student3 s = new Student3(name, chineseScore, mathScore, englishScore,s1.sumScore(chineseScore,mathScore,englishScore));
            treeSet.add(s);
        }
        for (Student3 student3 : treeSet) {
            System.out.println(student3);
        }
    }
}
~~~

> 2ã€ä¸€ä¸ªé”®å¯¹åº”ä¸€ä¸ªå€¼ï¼Œé”®ä¸å…è®¸é‡å¤ï¼Œé”®æ˜¯å”¯ä¸€çš„

##### 2ã€æˆå‘˜æ–¹æ³•ï¼ˆå®ç°çš„æ–¹å¼ï¼šé€šè¿‡å…·ä½“çš„å­ç±»HashMapï¼‰

> ```java

> V remove(Object key//è¿”å›åˆ é™¤é”®æ‰€å¯¹åº”çš„å€¼

###### 2.1ã€ä¸¾ä¾‹

~~~Java
public class MapDemo1 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        //åˆ›å»ºHashMapçš„å¯¹è±¡
        //HashMap()
        //æ„é€ ä¸€ä¸ªç©ºçš„ HashMap ï¼Œé»˜è®¤åˆå§‹å®¹é‡ï¼ˆ16ï¼‰å’Œé»˜è®¤è´Ÿè½½ç³»æ•°ï¼ˆ0.75ï¼‰ã€‚
        HashMap<Integer, String> map1 = new HashMap<>();

        //V put(K key,V value) å‘é›†åˆä¸­æ·»åŠ ä¸€ä¸ªå…ƒç´ é”®å€¼å¯¹ï¼Œå¦‚æœé”®å·²ç»å­˜åœ¨é›†åˆä¸­ï¼Œå€¼ä¼šè¿›è¡Œè¦†ç›–å¤„ç†ï¼Œè¿”å›è¢«è¦†ç›–çš„å€¼
        //å‘mapé›†åˆä¸­æ·»åŠ ä¸€ä¸ªé”®å€¼å¯¹å…ƒç´ 
        System.out.println(map1.put(1001, "å°šå¹³"));
        System.out.println("map1: " + map1);
        System.out.println("--------------------------------");
        System.out.println(map1.put(1001, "ä¸ä¹‰æ°"));
        System.out.println("map1: " + map1);
        System.out.println("--------------------------------");
        map1.put(1003, "ä¹”ä¸¹");
        map1.put(1002, "é»„æ°");
        map1.put(1004, "å¢é¹");
        map1.put(1005, "å¼ è·ƒ");
        System.out.println("map1: " + map1);
        System.out.println("--------------------------------");
        //V remove(Object key) æ ¹æ®é”®åˆ é™¤æ•´ä¸ªé”®å€¼å¯¹ï¼Œå› ä¸ºé”®æ˜¯å”¯ä¸€çš„ï¼Œè¿”å›é”®å¯¹åº”çš„å€¼
        System.out.println(map1.remove(1100));
        System.out.println("map1: " + map1);
//        System.out.println("--------------------------------");
//        //void clear()
//        map1.clear();
//        System.out.println("map1: " + map1);
        System.out.println("--------------------------------");
        //boolean containsKey(Object key)
        System.out.println(map1.containsKey(1001));
        //boolean containsValue(Object value)
        System.out.println(map1.containsValue("é»„æ°1"));
        System.out.println("--------------------------------");
        //boolean isEmpty()
        System.out.println(map1.isEmpty());
        System.out.println("--------------------------------");
        //int size() è·å–å…ƒç´ çš„ä¸ªæ•°ï¼Œé”®å€¼å¯¹çš„ä¸ªæ•°
        System.out.println(map1.size());




    }
}
~~~

###### 2.2ã€ä¸¾ä¾‹2

~~~Java
package com.shujia.day14;

import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Set;

/*
æˆå‘˜æ–¹æ³•ï¼š
    V get(Object key)
    Set<K> keySet()
    Collection<V> values()
    Set<Map.Entry<K,V>> entrySet()


    Mapé›†åˆéå†çš„æ–¹å¼ï¼š
        1ã€å…ˆè·å–æ‰€æœ‰çš„é”®ï¼Œéå†é”®è·å–å¯¹åº”çš„å€¼
        2ã€ç›´æ¥è·å–æ‰€æœ‰çš„é”®å€¼å¯¹ï¼Œéå†æ¯ä¸€ä¸ªé”®å€¼å¯¹ï¼Œå°±èƒ½å¤Ÿå¾—åˆ°æ¯ä¸€ä¸ªé”®å’Œå€¼
 */
public class MapDemo2 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        HashMap<Integer, String> map1 = new HashMap<>();
        map1.put(1001, "å°šå¹³");
        map1.put(1003, "ä¹”ä¸¹");
        map1.put(1002, "é»„æ°");
        map1.put(1004, "å¢é¹");
        map1.put(1005, "å¼ è·ƒ");
        System.out.println("map1: " + map1);
        System.out.println("-------------------------");
        //V get(Object key) æ ¹æ®é”®è·å–å€¼
        System.out.println(map1.get(1010));
        System.out.println("-------------------------");
        //Set<K> keySet() è·å–æ‰€æœ‰çš„é”®ç»„æˆä¸€ä¸ªSeté›†åˆè¿”å›
        Set<Integer> keySet = map1.keySet();
        System.out.println(keySet);
        System.out.println("-------------------------");
        //Collection<V> values()
        Collection<String> values = map1.values();
        System.out.println(values);
        System.out.println("-------------------------");
        //Set<Map.Entry<K,V>> entrySet()
        Set<Map.Entry<Integer, String>> entries = map1.entrySet();
        System.out.println(entries);

    }
}
~~~

##### 3ã€éå†çš„æ–¹æ³•

###### 3.1ã€å…ˆè·å–æ‰€æœ‰çš„é”®ï¼Œéå†é”®è·å–å¯¹åº”çš„å€¼

~~~Java
public class MapDemo3 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        HashMap<Integer, String> map1 = new HashMap<>();
        map1.put(1001, "å°šå¹³");
        map1.put(1003, "ä¹”ä¸¹");
        map1.put(1002, "é»„æ°");
        map1.put(1004, "å¢é¹");
        map1.put(1005, "å¼ è·ƒ");
        System.out.println("map1: " + map1);
        System.out.println("-------------------------");
        //è·å–æ‰€æœ‰çš„é”®
        Set<Integer> keySet = map1.keySet();
        for (Integer key : keySet) {
            //æ ¹æ®é”®è·å–å¯¹åº”çš„å€¼
            String value = map1.get(key);
            System.out.println(key + "--" + value);
        }
    }
}
~~~

###### 3.2ã€ç›´æ¥è·å–æ‰€æœ‰çš„é”®å€¼å¯¹ï¼Œéå†æ¯ä¸€ä¸ªé”®å€¼å¯¹ï¼Œå°±èƒ½å¤Ÿå¾—åˆ°æ¯ä¸€ä¸ªé”®å’Œå€¼

~~~Java
public class MapDemo4 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        HashMap<Integer, String> map1 = new HashMap<>();
        map1.put(1001, "å°šå¹³");
        map1.put(1003, "ä¹”ä¸¹");
        map1.put(1002, "é»„æ°");
        map1.put(1004, "å¢é¹");
        map1.put(1005, "å¼ è·ƒ");
        System.out.println("map1: " + map1);
        System.out.println("-------------------------");
        //å…ˆè·å–æ‰€æœ‰çš„é”®å€¼å¯¹
        Set<Map.Entry<Integer, String>> keyValues = map1.entrySet();
        for (Map.Entry<Integer, String> keyValue : keyValues) {
            Integer key = keyValue.getKey();
            String value = keyValue.getValue();
            System.out.println(key + "--" + value);
        }
    }
}
~~~



#### Mapæ¥å£-HashMapç±»

##### 1ã€æ¦‚è¿°

> é”®æ˜¯å“ˆå¸Œè¡¨ç»“æ„ï¼Œå¯ä»¥ä¿è¯é”®çš„å”¯ä¸€æ€§ï¼Œçº¿ç¨‹ä¸å®‰å…¨ï¼Œæ•ˆç‡é«˜

##### 2ã€æ¡ˆä¾‹

> åˆ›å»ºå­¦ç”Ÿç±»

~~~Java
package com.shujia.day14;

import java.util.Objects;

public class Student1{
    private String name;
    private int age;

    public Student1() {
    }

    public Student1(String name, int age) {
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
    }

    public String getName() {
        return name;
    }

    public void setName(String name) {
        this.name = name;
    }

    public int getAge() {
        return age;
    }

    public void setAge(int age) {
        this.age = age;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean equals(Object o) {
        if (this == o) return true;
        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) return false;
        Student1 student1 = (Student1) o;
        return age == student1.age && Objects.equals(name, student1.name);
    }

    @Override
    public int hashCode() {
        return Objects.hash(name, age);
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return "Student1{" +
                "name='" + name + '\'' +
                ", age=" + age +
                '}';
    }

//    @Override
//    public int compareTo(Student1 o) {
//        //æŒ‰ç…§å¹´é¾„ä»å°åˆ°å¤§æ’åº
//        int i1 = this.getAge() - o.getAge();
//        //éšè—æ¡ä»¶ï¼šå¹´é¾„ä¸€æ ·çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œå§“åä¸ä¸€å®šä¸€æ ·
//        return (i1 == 0) ? this.getName().compareTo(o.getName()) : i1;
//    }
}
~~~

> å®ç°

~~~Java
package com.shujia.day14;

import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Set;

/*
    æ ¹æ®æ˜¨å¤©HashSetä¸­addæ–¹æ³•å®é™…ä¸Šå°±æ˜¯è°ƒç”¨ä»Šå¤©è¦è®²çš„HashMapä¸­çš„putæ–¹æ³•ï¼Œè¦æƒ³ä¿è¯HashMapä¸­çš„é”®å”¯ä¸€
    æ ¹æ®åˆ†æå¾—å‡ºï¼Œé”®çš„ç±»å‹è¦é‡å†™hashCode()æ–¹æ³•å’Œequalsæ–¹æ³•

    HashMap<Student,String> å½“å­¦ç”Ÿçš„å§“åå’Œå¹´é¾„ä¸€æ ·çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œè®¤ä¸ºæ˜¯åŒä¸€ä¸ªå­¦ç”Ÿ

 */
public class HashMapDemo1 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        //åˆ›å»ºé›†åˆå¯¹è±¡
        HashMap<Student1, String> map = new HashMap<>();

        //åˆ›å»ºå…ƒç´ å¯¹è±¡
        Student1 s1 = new Student1("å°çº¢", 16);
        Student1 s2 = new Student1("å°çº¢2", 15);
        Student1 s3 = new Student1("å°çº¢3", 18);
        Student1 s4 = new Student1("å°çº¢4", 19);
        Student1 s5 = new Student1("å°çº¢", 16);

        //å‘é›†åˆä¸­æ·»åŠ å…ƒç´ 
        map.put(s1, "æ‰“ç¯®çƒ");
        map.put(s2, "è¸¢è¶³çƒ");
        map.put(s3, "æ‰“æ’çƒ");
        map.put(s4, "æ‰“å°çƒ");
        map.put(s5, "æ‰“ç¾½æ¯›çƒ");

        //éå†é›†åˆ
        Set<Map.Entry<Student1, String>> entries = map.entrySet();
        for (Map.Entry<Student1, String> entry : entries) {
            Student1 key = entry.getKey();
            String value = entry.getValue();
            System.out.println(key + ": " + value);
        }
    }
}
~~~

###### 2.2ã€æ¡ˆä¾‹2
