  - ~~~java
    public interface Inter2 {
        void fun1(int a,int b);
    }
    public class Demo1 {
        public static void main(String[] args) {
    		//éœ€æ±‚ï¼šæ¥å£ä¸­çš„é€»è¾‘æ±‚ä¸¤ä¸ªæ•°ç›¸ä¹˜çš„è¾“å‡º
            //TODO:ç»“è®º2ï¼šå½“æ¥å£çš„å‚æ•°å¤§äºç­‰äº2ä¸ªçš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œæ”¹å†™Lambdaè¡¨è¾¾å¼çš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œå·¦è¾¹å°æ‹¬å·ä¸å¯ä»¥çœç•¥
           	 show2(3, 4, (e1, e2) -> System.out.println(e1 * e2));
    //        show2(3, 4, (e1, e2) -> System.out.println(e1 + e2));
    //        show2(3, 4, (e1, e2) -> System.out.println(e1 - e2));
    //        show2(3, 4, (e1, e2) -> System.out.println(e1 / e2));
    ~~~

- è‹¥ Lambda ä½“ä¸­åªæœ‰ä¸€æ¡è¯­å¥ï¼Œ return å’Œ å¤§æ‹¬å·éƒ½å¯ä»¥çœç•¥ä¸å†™

  - åŸºæœ¬è¯­å¥æ ¼å¼
    (å˜é‡å1, å˜é‡å2) -> è¦è¿”å›çš„ç»“æœ;

  - ~~~java
    public interface Inter4 {
        String fun1(String s1, String s2);
    }        
    //éœ€æ±‚ï¼šå°†ä¸¤ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²è¿›è¡Œæ‹¼æ¥æ“ä½œï¼Œè¿”å›

##### 5ã€lambdaå†…ç½®å‡½æ•°å¼æ¥å£

###### 5.1ã€Predicate<T> æ–­è¨€å‹æ¥å£

```java
@FunctionalInterface
public interface Predicate<T> {
    boolean test(T t);
}
public class Staff {
    private String id;
    private String name;
    private int age;
    private int salary;

    public Staff() {
    }

    public Staff(String id, String name, int age, int salary) {
        this.id = id;
        this.name = name;
        this.age = age;
        this.salary = salary;
    }

    public String getId() {
        return id;
    }

    public void setId(String id) {
        this.id = id;
    }

    public String getName() {
        return name;
    }

    public void setName(String name) {
        this.name = name;
    }

    public int getAge() {
        return age;
    }

    public void setAge(int age) {
        this.age = age;
    }

    public int getSalary() {
        return salary;
    }

    public void setSalary(int salary) {
        this.salary = salary;
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return "Staff{" +
                "id='" + id + '\'' +
                ", name='" + name + '\'' +
                ", age=" + age +
                ", salary=" + salary +
                '}';
    }
}
/*
    æ¥å£ç±»å‹ï¼š
    @FunctionalInterface
    public interface Predicate<T> {
        boolean test(T t);
    }   

 */
public class Demo {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        //åˆ›å»ºä¸€ä¸ªå‘˜å·¥
        ArrayList<Staff> staffList = new ArrayList<>();
        staffList.add(new Staff("1001", "ä¸ä¹‰æ°", 22, 10000));
        staffList.add(new Staff("1002", "ä¸ä¹‰æ°1", 17, 3000));
        staffList.add(new Staff("1003", "ä¸ä¹‰æ°2", 24, 20000));
        staffList.add(new Staff("1004", "ä¸ä¹‰æ°3", 19, 1000));
        staffList.add(new Staff("1005", "ä¸ä¹‰æ°4", 16, 500));

        System.out.println("==================éœ€æ±‚1ï¼šè¿‡æ»¤å‡ºå¹´é¾„æ˜¯å¤§äº18å²çš„å‘˜å·¥é›†åˆ=======================");
        List<Staff> staffRes1 = filterStaff(staffList, e -> e.getAge() > 18);
        for (Staff staff : staffRes1) {
            System.out.println(staff);
        }

        System.out.println("==================éœ€æ±‚2ï¼šè¿‡æ»¤å‡ºè–ªèµ„æ˜¯å¤§äº2000çš„å‘˜å·¥é›†åˆ=======================");
        List<Staff> staffRes2 = filterStaff(staffList, e -> e.getSalary() > 2000);
        for (Staff staff : staffRes2) {
            System.out.println(staff);
        }
    }

    public static List<Staff> filterStaff(ArrayList<Staff> staffList, Predicate<Staff> predicate) {
        ArrayList<Staff> staffArrayList = new ArrayList<>();
        for (Staff staff : staffList) {
            if (predicate.test(staff)) {
                staffArrayList.add(staff);
            }
        }
        return staffArrayList;
    }
}
```

###### 5.2ã€Function<T,R> å‡½æ•°å‹æ¥å£

~~~Java
/*
    Function<T,R> å‡½æ•°å‹æ¥å£

    @FunctionalInterface
    public interface Function<T, R> {
        R apply(T t);
    }

 */
public class Demo {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s = show("å°šå¹³", e -> "æ•°åŠ ï¼š" + e);

        System.out.println(s);
    }

    public static String show(String s, Function<String, String> function) {
        return function.apply(s);
    }
}
~~~

###### 5.3ã€Supplier<T> ä¾›ç»™å‹æ¥å£

~~~Java
/*
    ä¾›ç»™å‹æ¥å£
    @FunctionalInterface
    public interface Supplier<T> {
        T get();
    }

    éšæœºç”Ÿæˆ10ä¸ª1-100çš„æ•°æ®åˆ°é›†åˆè¿”å›


 */
public class Demo2 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        List<Integer> integerList = getNumber(() -> (int) (Math.random() * 100 + 1));
        for (Integer i : integerList) {
            System.out.println(i);
        }
    }

    public static List<Integer> getNumber(Supplier<Integer> supplier) {
        ArrayList<Integer> arrayList = new ArrayList<>();

        for (int i = 1; i <= 10; i++) {
            Integer n = supplier.get();
            arrayList.add(n);
        }

        return arrayList;
    }
}
~~~

###### 5.4Consumer<T> æ¶ˆè´¹å‹æ¥å£

~~~Java
/*
    æ¶ˆè´¹å‹æ¥å£

    @FunctionalInterface
    public interface Consumer<T> {
        void accept(T t);
    }

 */
public class Demo3 {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        show(10,e-> System.out.println(e));
    }

    public static void show(int i, Consumer<Integer> consumer) {
        consumer.accept(i);
    }
}
~~~

##### 6ã€Lambdaç”¨æ³•å†ç®€æ´ä¹‹æ–¹æ³•å¼•ç”¨

      private String name;

      }

      }

          this.name = name;

###### 6.4ã€æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•å¼•ç”¨ ClassName::new

##### 8ã€ä¼˜ç¼ºç‚¹

  å¯ä»¥å‡å°‘ä»£ç çš„ä¹¦å†™ï¼Œå‡å°‘åŒ¿åå†…éƒ¨ç±»çš„åˆ›å»ºï¼ŒèŠ‚çœå†…å­˜å ç”¨ã€‚
  ä½¿ç”¨æ—¶ä¸ç”¨å»è®°å¿†æ‰€ä½¿ç”¨çš„æ¥å£å’ŒæŠ½è±¡å‡½æ•°ã€‚

  ä¸æ–¹ä¾¿è¿›è¡Œè°ƒè¯•ã€‚

#### ç¬¬åä¸€ç« æšä¸¾

##### 1ã€æ¦‚è¿°

- æšä¸¾ç±»å‹æ˜¯Javaä¸­ä¸€ç§ç”¨äºç»Ÿä¸€ç®¡ç†æœ‰é™çš„å¸¸é‡æ•°æ®çš„æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ã€‚å®ƒå°†å¸¸é‡è®¾ç½®ä¸ºå¯¹è±¡ï¼Œæé«˜äº†ä»£ç çš„å¯è¯»æ€§å’Œç®€æ´æ€§ã€‚é€šè¿‡ä½¿ç”¨æšä¸¾ç±»å‹ï¼Œå¯ä»¥åœ¨ä»£ç ä¸­æ›´æ–¹ä¾¿åœ°è¯»å–å’Œä½¿ç”¨å¸¸é‡

##### 2ã€JDK1.5ä¹‹å‰çš„æšä¸¾

          Season spring = Season.SPRING;
          System.out.println(spring);
  
      }
  }
  
  //åœ¨JDK1.5ä¹‹å‰ï¼Œäººä»¬å»ç¼–å†™ä¸€ä¸ªæšä¸¾ç±»çš„å®ç°
  class Season{
      //1. åˆ›å»ºæšä¸¾ç±»çš„å±æ€§(æˆå‘˜å˜é‡)ï¼Œå¿…é¡»æ˜¯ä½œä¸ºç§æœ‰å¸¸é‡å‡ºç°
      private String name;
      private String info;
  
      //2. å¿…é¡»å°†æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•ç§æœ‰åŒ–ï¼Œè¿™æ˜¯ä¸ºäº†ä¿è¯ç±»çš„å¯¹è±¡æ˜¯æœ‰é™ä¸ªçš„ç›®çš„
      private Season(String name,String info){
          this.name = name;
          this.info = info;
      }
  
  
      //3. æä¾›å…¬å…±çš„é™æ€çš„finalæ–¹æ³•ç»™å¤–ç•Œè·å–æšä¸¾ç±»ä¸­å¤šä¸ªå¯¹è±¡
      public static final Season SPRING = new Season("æ˜¥å¤©","æ˜¥æš–èŠ±å¼€");
      public static final Season SUMMER = new Season("å¤å¤©","å¤æ—¥ç‚ç‚");
      public static final Season AUTUMN = new Season("ç§‹å¤©","ç§‹é«˜æ°”çˆ½");
      public static final Season WINTER = new Season("å†¬å¤©","é“¶è£…ç´ è£¹");
  
      //4. æä¾›å…¬å…±çš„è·å–å±æ€§çš„æ–¹æ³•
      public String getName() {
          return name;
      }
  
      public String getInfo() {
          return info;
      }
  
      //5. é‡å†™toString()æ–¹æ³•
      @Override
      public String toString() {
          return "Season{" +
                  "name='" + name + '\'' +
                  ", info='" + info + '\'' +
                  '}';
      }
  }

##### 3ã€JDK1.5ä¹‹åçš„æšä¸¾

  interface Inter{

              System.out.println("å¥½å¥½å­¦ä¹ ï¼Œå¤©å¤©å‘ä¸Šï¼");

              System.out.println("åƒæ°´æœ");
